ʻAki ʻa e foʻi fakakaukau ko iá, ʻe malava ke ikuna ʻa Misa Trump ʻa e toe fili ʻo e 2020, tukukehe, ʻo hangē koe fakaʻamu ʻa e kau lipeloló, ke fakangata taʻekakato ʻene tuʻunga fakapalesitení ki ha ngaahi faihala pe angataʻetaau.
ʻO ʻikai ha toe tālaʻa "Ko e fakaʻosinga longoaʻa lahi taha ʻo ha palesiteni!"
ʻI he taimi ní, ʻoku ʻikai ha toe fakaʻilonga ʻo ha mamata ongoongosia.
Talu meí he 2014, lahi ʻo e taimi kamatá ne lahi ange ai ʻa e liunga ua ki he 1.05 miliona ʻi he CNN pea meimei liunga tolu ki he 1.6 miliona ʻi he MSNBC.
Kuo ʻi ai ha ʻavalisi ʻe 2.4 miliona ʻa e Fox News ki he kau fuofua mamatá, ʻo aʻu ki he 1.7 miliona ʻi he taʻu ʻe fā kuo hilí, fakatatau kia Nielsen, pea ko e MSNBC'S "The Rachel Maddow Show" kuo ne tuʻu meiʻolunga ʻi ha lahi fakakeipolo mo ha kakai tokolahi kuo aʻu ki he kau mamata ʻe 3.5 miliona ʻi he ngaahi faiʻanga ongoongo lalahí.
"Ko e afi ʻeni ʻoku ne tohoakiʻi mai ʻa e kakaí koeʻuhi ʻoku ʻikai ko ha meʻa ia ʻoku tau mahinoʻi," pehē ʻe Neal Baer, ko ha polokalama ʻoku fakalele ʻe he ABC drama "Designated Survivor," kau ki ha sekelitali kapineti ne hoko ko ha palesiteni hili ha fakatamaki ʻo ne fakaʻauha ʻa e Kolomuʻá.
Ne tohi ha faʻu tohi fakakata ka ko e faʻutohi ʻo e "Just the Funny Parts (Ko e Ngaahi Konga Fakaolí): And a Few Hard Truths About Sneaking Into the Hollywood Boys (Mo ha Ngaahi Meʻa Siʻi Fekauʻaki mo e Hola ki he Tamaiki Tangata ʻo Hollywood" Kalapu," ʻoku ai ha toe fakakaukau.
ʻOku ne kei manatuʻi ha heka kā ʻi Boston ki muʻa ʻi he fiil ʻo e 2016.
Ne talaange ʻe he fakaʻulí te ne fili kia Misa Trump.
Ko e hā ho ʻuhingá? naʻá ne fehuʻi.
"Naʻá ne pehē, "Koeʻuhi ʻoku ne ʻai au keu kata,"" ne talamai ʻe Ms. Scovell .
ʻOku ʻi ai ha tefitoʻi ʻulungaanga fakafiefia ʻi he faingataʻá.
Ko ia, ʻo ʻikai tatau mo ha meʻa kehe ʻi he Televīsoné, ko e ngaahi ʻuluʻi talanoa ʻoku haʻu mei Washington te ne lava ʻo tala ʻa e kahaʻu ʻo Roe v. Wade, ʻo tatau ai pē pe ʻe toe lava ke fakatahaʻi ʻa e ngaahi fāmili hikifonuá pea moe ʻekonomika fakamāmani lahí pea mo e moʻui leleí.
Hū ki tuʻa ko ha moʻui tuʻumālie ko e kau mamata matuʻaki tuʻumālie pē te nau lava ʻo kumí.
Ka ʻi he lolotongá, ʻoku hoko atu ʻo ope ki he kakai nofo fonua kuo nau ʻilo ki aí ʻi he aʻu ki ha houa ʻe ono hoʻo mamata ʻi ha pēnolo ʻo ha kau mataotao ne fakakikihi ʻe Bob Woodward ʻa e ngāueʻaki ʻo e "puiuituʻa lolotó" mei heʻene tohi ko e "Fear," mo e saketi leta $15,000 ʻa Paul Manafort ("ko ha vala ʻoku fakamatolu ʻaki ʻa e taʻetokaʻí," fakahā ia ʻe he The Washington Post) pea mo e fokotuʻu ʻo e fakamatala ʻa Stormy Daniel kau ki he natula ʻo Mr. Trump.
Ko au, heʻikai pē ke toe tatau ʻeku sio kia Mario.
"Ko e konga ʻo e meʻa ʻoku ne fakahoko ʻoku ne ngaohi koe ke ke ongoʻi ʻoku ke ʻi ha polokalama tv moʻoni ʻo hangē ʻoku ne fafanga koe ʻi he poʻulí," fakamatala ia ʻa Brent Montgomery, ko e pule maʻolunga ʻo e Wheelhouse Entertainment pea mo e tangata faʻu ʻo e "Pawn Stars," kau ki ha he polokalama TV ʻa Trump ʻa ia ʻoku fetongitongi ai ʻa e kau fai polokalamá pea mo e ngaahi liliu ʻi he fakamatalá(kamataʻi ha tau pea mo e N.F.L., fakahikihikiʻi ʻa Kim Jong-un).
ʻOku ʻikai fiemaʻu ke ke taʻesio ʻi ha konga ʻe taha naʻá ke tomui.
ʻI heʻeku aʻu ki Misa Fleiss ʻi he uike ní, ne laʻā tikilī ʻe 80 ʻa tuʻa ʻi hono ʻapí ʻi he tokelau ʻo Kauai, ka naʻe ʻi loto ia ʻo fai ʻene sio MSNBC lolotonga ia ʻene hiki ʻi he CNN..
Neʻikai ke ne lava ʻo toʻo ia, ʻikai lava koeʻuhi ko e fokotuʻu ʻo Brett Kavanaugh ke fehangahangai mo e Komiti Fakamaau ʻa e Senatoá pea moe kahaʻu ʻo e Fakamaau Lahí.
"ʻOku ou manatuʻi ʻi he lolotonga ʻemau fakahoko ʻa e ngaahi polokalama taʻefakakaukauʻi ʻi he fuoloá pea pehē leva ʻe he kakaí "Ko e kamataʻanga ʻeni ʻo e ngataʻanga ʻo e fakalakalaka FakaUēsité,"" ne talamai ʻe Mr. Fleiss.
"Ne u fakakaukau ko ha fakakata pē, ka ne hoko ia ʻo moʻoni."
Ne tohi ʻe Amy Chozick, ko ha fefine faʻu tohi maʻá e The Times ʻi he tafaʻaki fakapisinisí, politikí, mo e mītiá, ko e faʻu tohi ʻo e "Chasing Hillary."
ʻI tuʻa ʻoku tafea paʻanga ki he fili vaeuaʻanga teemi fetohotohoi ʻi he Falé
ʻOku ʻikai fakaofo ʻa e tafea ʻo e paʻangá ʻi Pennsylvania fika 17, mālō ki he feliliuaki ʻi he ngaahi vahenga fakapuleʻanga ʻa ia naʻe hoko ai ha ongo maʻu lakanga ʻi he lova ki he nofoʻanga tatau.
Ne toe hu ʻa e fakafofonga Temokalati ʻo e vahe Pittsurg, Conor Lamb - ʻa ia naʻá ne iku na hono nofoʻangá ʻi ha fili fakavahe ʻi he taʻu kuoʻosí.
ʻOku toe lele pē ʻa Lamb mo ha taha maʻu lakanga meí he tafaʻaki ʻa e Lepapuliká ko Keith Rorthfus, ʻa ia ʻokú ne lolotonga fakafofongaʻi ʻa Pennsylvania vahenga 12, ʻa ia ʻoku aʻu mai ia ki he fika 17 foʻoú.
Ne toe tā foʻou ʻa e ngaah mapé hili ʻa e tuʻutuʻuni ʻa e Fakamaauʻanga Lahi ʻo Pennsylvania ʻi Sanuali ʻo pehē ko e vahe motuʻá ne taʻefakakonisitūtone ia ʻi he fiemaʻu ʻa e Kau Lepapuliká.
Ko e lova ʻi he fika 17 kuó ne fakahoko ha feʻauʻauhi ʻi he kemipeini fakapaʻanga ʻi he vahaʻa ʻo e paati fakapaʻangá, ko e Democratic Campaign Congressional Committee (DCCC) pea mo e National Republican Campaign Committee (NRCC).
Kuo hoko ʻa Lamb ko ha hingoa ʻiloa ʻi Pennsylvania hili ʻa e ikuna ʻi hano mamataʻi tokolahi ʻi he fili makehe ʻi Maʻasi maʻá e Vahenga Fakapuleʻanga fika 18 ʻa Pennsylvania.
Ko ha nofoʻanga ne ʻi ha taha Lepapulika ʻi ha ngaahi taʻu ʻe hongofulu tupu, pea ko Palesiteni Donald Trump naʻá ne ikuna ʻa e fili ʻi he vahenga ko iá ʻaki ʻa e poini ko e 20.
Kuo ʻoange ʻe he kaku mataotao fakapolitikalé ha kiʻi faingamālie maʻá e kau Temokalatí.
Puleʻanga ʻAmeliká Kuo tauteaʻi ʻa El Salvador koeʻuhi Ko ha Poupou ki Siaina, Pea Nau Mavahe
Ne fakatokangaʻi ʻe he kau tipilomētiká ʻa e Dominican Republic mo Panama ʻa ʻena fakaʻiloʻilo ki Beijing, pea mo ha kiʻi teke ki mui mei Washington.
Ne ʻi ai ha fakataha mafana ʻa Misa Trump pea mo e Palesiteni ʻo Panama ko Juan Carlos Varela ʻi Sune 2017 pea ʻi ai ha hotele ʻi Panama ki muʻa pea fetukutuku ʻa e timi ʻo e Kautaha ngāue ʻa Trump.
Ne fakakaukau ʻa e Vaʻa Siteití ke ui fakafoki ʻa e kau pule ngāue fakatipilometika ʻa ʻAmeliká mei El Salvador, mo e Dominican Republic pea mo Panama hili ʻa e "ngaahi tuʻutuʻuni fakamuimui taha ke ʻoua naʻa toe ʻo hake ʻa Taiwan," ko e fakamatala ia ʻa Heather Nauert ko e fakafofonga vaʻa ngāue, ʻi he māhiná ni.
Ka koe ngaahi tautea ne fakakaukau ke fakahoko pē ia ki El Savador, ʻa ia ʻoku ne maʻu ha fakafuofua ʻo ha $140 miliona meí he tokoni ʻa ʻAmeliká ʻi he 2017, kau ki ai mo ʻenau tokoni ki hono tauʻi e faitoʻo konatapú, langa fakalakalaka mo fakaʻekonōmika.
Ko e ngaahi fokotuʻu tauteá, ʻa ia ne kau ki ai ʻa hono tuʻusi ʻo e ngaahi tokoni fakapaʻangaá pea mo e fakangatangata ʻo e foaki visa, ne mei faingataʻa ki he fonua ko ʻeni ʻi ʻAmelika Lotolotó pea mo ʻene kau taʻemaʻungāue tuʻunga maʻolungá pehe ki he tāmate tuʻunga maʻolungá.
ʻI ha fakataha ne fakahoko fakalotofonua, ne toloai ai ʻe he kau ʻofisa maʻolunga ʻo ʻAmelika Tokelaú pea mo ʻAmelika Lotolotó ʻa e konifelenisi mahuʻingá ni ʻa ia ne fakatefito ʻihe malu mo e tuʻumālie fakaʻekonōmiká ke muimuiʻi ha fakatahaʻanga tatau mo e taʻu kuo ʻosí ne hoko ko ha sitepu ki muʻa ʻi he feinga ke fakangata ʻa e ʻa e kau hikifonuá mei heʻenau taumuʻa atu ki he United States.
Ka ʻi he aʻu ki he vaeuaʻanga ʻo Sepitemá, ne fakamahinoʻi ʻe he kau taki maʻolungá ne nau fiemaʻu ʻa e konifelenisi ke laka ki muʻa, pea fakaʻosinga lelei kau ki ha tautea ne fokotuʻu maʻa El Salvador.
Kuo vahe ki he Tokoni Palesiteni ko Mike Pence ke lea ʻi he konifelenisí, kuo fokotuʻuia ki he konga ki loto ʻo ʻOkatopá, ʻi ha fakaʻilonga ki he hū mai ʻo e ngaahi feituʻu maʻolunga ki he fakatahaʻangá, ne pehē ʻe he kau tipilomētiká.
Pea ne foki fakalongolongo ʻa e kau fakafofonga ʻAmelika ʻe toko tolú meí El Salvador, Panama pea mo e Dominican Republic ʻo ʻikai ha pōpoaki fefeka pe tautea mei Washington.
Ne ʻikai ke ʻi ai ha lau ʻa Misa Bolton ko e fakafofonga ʻo e White House ki he fakaikiiki ʻo e fakakikihí ʻa ia ne fakamatalaʻi ʻe he kau ʻofisa maʻolunga ʻe toko tolú, ʻa ia ne nau loto ke aleaʻi ʻa e ngaahi tuʻutuʻuni fakalotofonuá ʻi he tukunga ʻo e meʻa kuo hokó.
Ne fakatahaʻi ʻenau fakamatalá ʻe ha taha ʻanalaiso ʻi tuʻa ʻa ia ʻokú ne ofi ki he kau takí pea naʻá ne talanoa kau ki he tuʻunga ʻo e mea ʻoku hokó.
Hisitōlia ʻo e Akó
Ko e sū hoko ke fakatookí ʻe hangēhangē koe tokoni makehe ʻi he lipooti ʻa Robert Mueller fekauʻaki mo ha faingamālie ka hoko ke taʻofi ʻa e fakamaau totonú ʻe Mr. Trump, ʻa ia ʻoku ʻi ai fakamoʻoni lahi ʻi he lekooti fakapuleʻangá.
Kuo liooti ʻa Mr. Mueller ki hano fakatafoki ʻene fakatotoló ke sio pē koe kemipeini ʻa Mr. Trump ʻoku fepaki mo Russia ʻi heʻene ʻohofi ʻo ʻemau filí.
ʻOka liliu nima ʻa e Puleʻangá, ʻe fehangahangai ʻa Mr. Trump mo ha fatongia ʻi he sino ko iá, ʻo hangē ko ʻene teuteu ke toe ʻasi ʻi muʻa ʻi he kau filí, pea mahalo ʻe iku ki ha sula hono ngaahi kaungāmeʻá.
Ko ha ngaahi kapau lahi moʻoni ia, pea ʻoku ʻikai ke u ʻuhinga ke fokotuʻu atu ʻoku ko e tō ʻa Mr. Trump ʻe pau ʻene hokó - hangē ko mea tatau ʻou hoko ʻi ʻIulopé.
ʻOku ʻi ai ha ngaahi fili ke fakahoko ʻe kitautolu kotoa ʻi he ongo fahaʻí ʻo e ʻAtalanitiká, ʻa ia te ne uesia ʻa e fuoloa ʻo e faingataʻa ʻe malava ke hokó.
ʻI he 1938, ne maau ʻa e kau ʻofisa Siamané ke kamataʻi ha fakamoveuveu kia Hitler, ʻoka pau pē ne ʻikai tali ia ʻe he Uēsité pea poupouʻi ʻa e kau Sesilōvākiá ne ʻi Munich.
Ne tau tō, pea mole ʻa e faingamālie ke fakamamaʻo ʻa e ngaahi taʻu ne tamateʻi ai e kakai tokolahí ne hoko atu aí.
Ko e halanga ʻo e ngaahi makatuʻunga ʻo e hisitōliá ne takaiʻi ʻe ha ngaahi liliu poini, pea mo e faingataʻa ke taʻofi ʻa e laka atu, kaka ki ʻolunga, mo e toloi ʻo e temokalatí.
ʻOku fepaki ʻa ʻAmelika mo e ngaahi poini fetongi tuʻunga ʻi he taimí ni.
Ko e hā te tau fai kapau ne tuli ʻe Mr. Trump ʻa e Tokoni ʻAtoni Seniale ko Rod Rosenstein, ko e tangata naʻá ne puleʻi ʻa e ikuʻanga ʻo e fakatotolo ʻo Mr. Mueller?
Kuo ʻi he loto vai mafaná ʻa Resenstein talu mei hono lipooti ʻe he pepá ni, ʻi he taʻu kuoʻosí, naʻá ne fokotuʻu fakafūfū ke lekooti ʻa e palesitení pea mo e fakamahamahalo ki heʻene taʻetaau mo e lakangá.
Naʻe pehē ʻe Mr. Rosenstein ʻoku ʻikai tonu ʻa e fakamatalá.
"Te tau tali fēfē ki he kole foʻou ki he fakatotolo ʻa e FBI kia Brett Kavanaugh ʻoku ʻikai palanisi ia - pe kuo fakapapauʻi ki he Fakamaauʻanga Lahí neongo ʻa e moʻoni ʻa e talatalaaki ʻo e ʻohofi taʻetaaú pea mo e fakamoʻoni taʻefaitotonú?
Pea mahulu haké, te tau fili nai ʻi he vaeuaʻi teemí ki ha Fale Alea te ne ʻekeʻi ʻa e fakamaau totonú meí a Mr. Trump?
Kapau te atu tō ʻi he ngaahi sivi ko iá, ʻe toe maʻu loloa atu e nofo ʻa e temokalatí ʻi ha faʻahitaʻu momoko fuoloa.
Ka ʻoku ou tui ʻe ʻikai te tau tō, koeʻuhi koe lesoni ne u ako ʻi Prague.
Ko ʻeku faʻeé ko ha Siu Sesilōvakia ne tipotaʻi ki Auschwitz ʻi he taimi tatau ʻo e pule ʻa e kau Nazi ʻa ia ne ʻi ai ha taimi ne nau nofo ʻi hoku ʻapi fakaʻamipasitoá.
Naʻá ne moʻui, hikifonua ki ʻAmelika pea, ʻi ha taʻu ʻe 60 hili iá, naʻá ne ʻave au ke u tutu ʻa e teʻelango Sāpaté ʻi he funga tēpile ne ʻi ai ʻa e suasitiká.
ʻI heʻene hoko ko hoku tukufakaholó, ʻe anga fēfē ha ʻikai ke u fiefia fekauʻaki mo e kahaʻú?"
Ko Norman Eisen, ko ha taha maʻolunga ia ʻi he Ngāueʻanga Brookings, ko ia ʻa e sea ʻo e Kakai Nofo Fonua ki he Fatongiá mo e ʻEfiká ʻi Washington pea koe faʻu ia ʻo e tohi ko e "The Last Palace: Senituli Faingataʻa Maʻa ʻIulope ʻi ha Moʻui ʻe Nima mo e Fale Motuʻa ʻe Taha."
Tuʻamelia ʻa Graham Dorrans ʻo e Rangers ki he meʻa ʻe hoko ʻi he tau mo e Rapid Viena
Ne talitali ʻe he Rangers ʻa e Rapid Viena ʻi he ʻaho Tuʻapulelulú, ne nau ʻiloʻi ko ʻenau ikuna ʻi he kau ʻOsitulīá, ʻi heʻenau mahanga mo Spain ʻi heʻenau tau mo Villarreal ʻi he kamtaʻanga ʻo e māhiná, ʻe fokotuʻu ai kinautolu ʻi ha tuʻunga mālohi ke nau lava ai meí he Kulupu G ʻo e Liiki ʻa ʻIulopé.
Ne fakafaingataʻaʻiaʻi ʻe he lavea e tui ʻo e mitifila ko Graham Dorrans mei heʻene fakahoko ʻene fuofua hā ʻi he faʻahitaʻú tukukehe ʻa ʻena mahangá 2-2 mo Villareal ka naʻá ne tui ʻe lava ʻe he Rangers ʻo ngāueʻaki ʻa e ola ko iá ko ha teuteuʻanga ki ha ngaahi meʻa lelei.
"Ko ha poini lelei ia kia mautolu koeʻuhi ko Villarreal ko ha tafaʻaki lelei ia," ko e lau ia ʻa e taʻu 31.
"Ne mau ō ki he taú mo e tui te mau lava ʻo maʻu ha meá pea ne mau foki mai mo ha poini.
Mahalo pē ne mau mei ʻai ha kai ʻi he fakaʻosí ka, ʻi he fakakātoá, ne hoko ʻa e mahangá ko ha ola lelei pe ia.
Ne nau sai ʻi he ʻuluaki tuʻú pea mau sai mautolu ʻi he tuʻu hono uá.
ʻI he ʻalu atu ki he Tuʻapulelulú, ko ha toe pō lahi ia maʻa ʻIulope.
Fakaʻamu pē, te mau lava ʻo maʻu ha poini ʻe tolu ka ko ha vaʻinga ia ʻe faingataʻa koeʻuhi ne ʻi ai ʻenau ola lelei ʻi he tau ne toki ʻosí ka, ʻi heʻemau maʻu ʻa e matangá, ʻoku ou tui te mau lava ʻo teke pea maʻu mo ha ola lelei.
Ne matuʻaki faingataʻa pe ʻa e taʻu kuoʻosí, ʻi he vahaʻa ʻo e meʻa kotoa pē ne hokó ʻi heʻeku laveá pea mo e ngaahi liliu ʻi he kalapú ka ʻoku ʻi ai ha ongoʻi lelei ki he feituʻú ʻi he taimí ni.
ʻOku lelei ʻa e timí pea ʻoku fiefia ʻa e kau vaʻinga tangatá; ʻoku lelei mo e ako vaʻingá.
Tui pe, te mau lava ʻo teke ʻi he taimí ni, tuku atu ʻa e faʻahitaʻu vaʻingá ki mui pea hoko ʻo lavameʻa."
‘Ikai lava e kakai fefiné ʻo moh e koeʻuhi ko e manavahē ki hono tānaki ʻo e paʻanga vahenga mālōloó
Neongo ne moʻoni ʻa e ne maʻu ʻehe niʻihi ne kau ki he saveá ha fakakaukau maama ki he founga ne nau fiemaʻu ke tauhi ʻaki kinautolú, ne ʻi ai ha tokosiʻi ne talanoa ki he mēmipa honau ngaahi fāmilí fekauʻaki mo ia.
Meimei ko e vaeua ʻo e niʻihi ʻi he ako Fakamāmani Lahí ne nau talanoa mo honau ngaahi malí kau ki he totongi ʻo e tauhi taimi lōloá.
Ko e peseti ʻe 10 ne nau talanoa ki heʻenau fanaú fekauʻaki mo ia.
"ʻOku fiemaʻu ʻe he kakaí ha mēmipa ʻo honau fāmilí ke tokangaʻi kinautolu, ka ʻoku ʻikai ke nau fakahoko ha meʻa ke fai ai ha talanoa," ko Holly Snyder ia, ko e tokoni palesiteni ʻo e pisinisi maluʻi moʻui Fakamāmani Lahi.
Ko e founga ʻeni ke kamata aí.
Talanoa ki ho malí pea mo hoʻo fānaú: ʻE ʻikai te ke lava ʻo teuteuʻi ho fāmilí ke nau tokanga ʻo kapau ʻoku ʻikai ke ke fakahā ho ngaahi fakaʻamú ke nau ʻilo ki muʻa ki ai.
Ngāue mo ho fai faleʻí pea mo hoʻo fāmilí ke aleaʻi ʻa e feituʻu mo e founga ke maʻu ai ha tauhi, he ko e ngaahi fili ko iá te nau hoko ko ha ngaahi ʻuuni meʻa mahuʻinga ʻi hono fakapapauʻi ʻa e mahuʻingá.
ʻOmai ki ai hoʻo fai faleʻi fakapaʻangá: ʻE lava ho fai faleʻí ʻo tokoniʻi ko e ke ke faʻu ha founga ke totongi ai ʻa e ngaahi fakamole ko iá.
Ko hoʻo ngaahi fili tokoni fakapaʻanga ki ha tauhi taimi loloa te ne lava ke fakakau ha tuʻutuʻuni maluʻi ki ha tauhi taimi lōloa, faounga ohi ki ha tuʻutuʻuni maluʻi moʻui ʻoku mahuʻinga fakapaʻanga ke fakakakato ʻaki ʻa e ngaahi fakamolé pe ko ha maluʻi fakaefoʻituitui ʻaki ho paʻangá - ʻi he taimi kotoa pē ʻoku ke maʻu ai ʻa e paʻangá.
Ngāueʻi hoʻo ngaahi fakamoʻoni pepa fakalaó: Ngāueʻi ʻa e ngaahi feinga fakalao ʻi he kuohilí.
ʻOmi ha fakafofonga tauhi moʻui ke maau koeʻuhi ke ke fili ha taha falalaʻanga ke ne tokangaʻi hoʻo meʻa fakafaitoʻó, pea fakapapauʻi ʻoku muimui ʻa e kau ngāue fakapalofesinalé ki hoʻo ngaahi fiemaʻú koeʻuhi naʻa ʻikai keke lava ke fetuʻutaki.
Pea, fakakaukau ki he ivi ʻo e loea ki hoʻo ngaahi meʻa fakapaʻangá.
Te ke fili ha taha falalaʻanga ke fakahoko ʻa e ngaahi fili fakapaʻangá maʻá u pea mo fakapapauʻi ʻoku totongi hoʻo ngaahi moʻuá kapau ʻikai te ke malava.
ʻOua naʻa ngalo ʻa e ngaahi meʻa iikí: Fakakaukauloto ʻoku ʻi ai ha ngaahi fiemaʻu fakavavevave fakafaitoʻo ʻa hoʻo mātuʻa toulekeleká pea ʻoku leleakiʻi ki falemahaki.
Te ke lava nai ʻo tali ʻa e ngaahi fehuʻi ʻi he faitoʻó pea mo e puke ngofua tuʻunga ʻi ha meʻakai, fulufulu, pe efuefu ʻakau?
Tohiʻi  ʻa e ngaahi fakaikiiki ko iá ʻi ha palani ʻoku tohi koeʻuhi ke ke mateuteu.
"ʻOku ʻikai ko e ngaahi meʻa fakapaʻangá pē ʻoku fiemaʻú, ko hai ʻena kau toketaá?" ne fehuʻi ʻe Martin.
"Ko e hā ʻa e ngaahi faitoʻó?
Ko hai ʻe tokanga ki he kulií?
Teuteu e palaní ke maau."
Ne fanaʻi tuʻo lahi ha tangata ʻaki ha laifolo ʻi Ilfracombe
Kuo fanaʻi tuʻo lahi ha tangata ʻaki ha laifolo ʻea ʻi haʻane lue ki hono ʻapí hili haʻá ne ʻeva poʻuli.
Ne ʻi he ʻēlia Oxford Grove ʻo Ilfracombe ʻa e tangata taʻu 40 ni, ʻi he taimi naʻe fanaʻi aí ʻi hono fatafatá, keté pea mo e nimá.
Ne fakamatala ʻe he kau polisí ʻa e faná ʻa ia naʻe fakahoko ia fakaofi ki he 02:30 BST, ʻo pehē ko ha "fana noaʻia."
Ne ʻikai sio ʻa e mamahí ki he taha naʻá ne fai ʻa e fakamamahí.
ʻE ʻikai fakatupunga ʻe he ngaahi laveá ha mate pea kuo kole atu ai ʻe he kau polisí ha kau fakamoʻoni.
Mofuike mo e peaukula ʻi Indonesia
Ne ʻi he kakai ʻe toko 384 ne nau mate ʻi ha mofuike malohi pea mo ha peaukula naʻá ne hake ʻi he kolo ko Palú ʻi ʻInitonēsia ʻi he ʻaho Falaité, ne pehē ʻe he kau ʻofisa maʻolungá ʻoku ʻamanaki ke fakautuutu ʻa e tokolahi ʻo e kau pekiá.
ʻI he motuhia ʻa e fetuʻutakí, kuo teʻeki lava ʻa e kau ʻofisá ke maʻu ha faʻahinga fakamatala mei he puleʻanga Donggala, ko ha ʻēlia ʻi he fakatokelau ʻo Palu ʻa ia ʻoku ofi ki he uhouhonga ʻo e mofuike ne mekinitute 7.5
ʻI Palú, kuo fetukutuku ha kakai ne laka hake ʻi he toko 16,000 hili ʻa e hoko e fakatamakí.
Ko e ngaahi meʻa moʻoni eni fekauʻaki mo Palu mo Donggala, ʻi he motu ʻo Sulawesi:
Ko Palu ko e kolomuʻa ia ʻo e vahefonua Sulawesi Lotolotó, ʻa ia ʻoku tuʻu ʻi he tuliki fangaʻuta ʻo e hala tahi hihifo ʻo e motu ko Sulawesi, mo ha tokolahi ʻo ha kakai ʻoku fakafuofua k he toko 379,800 ʻi he 2017.
Ne kātoangaʻi ʻe he koló ʻa e fakamanatua hono taʻu 40 ʻi he taimi ne tō ai e peaukulá.
Ko Donggala ko ha puleʻanaga ʻoku ne kapui ʻo laka hake ʻi he kilomita ʻe 300 (maile 180) ʻi he matāfanga ʻo e fakatokelau hihifo ʻo e motu ko Sulawesi.
Ko e puleʻangá, ʻoku puleʻi ʻe ha kau taki ʻoku taupotu ki ha vahefonua, ne aʻu hono tokolahí ki he toko 299,200 ʻi he 2017.
Ko e maʻuʻanga moʻui tefito ʻo Sulawesi Lotolotó ko e toutai mo e ngoue, tautefito ki he matāfanga ʻo Donggala.
ʻOku mahuʻinga mo e keli maka nikoló ʻi he vahefonuá, ka ʻoku lahi fakatefito pe ʻi Morowali, ʻi he tafaʻaki ʻe taha ʻo e matāfanga ʻo Sulawesi.
Kuo lahi ha ngaahi taimi kuo hake ai ʻa e peaukulá ʻi Donggala ʻi he ngaahi taʻu ʻe 100 kuo hilí, ʻo fakatatau ki he Kautaha Tokangaekina ʻo e Fakatamaki ʻa Indonesia.
ʻI he taʻu 1938, ne tamateʻi ai ʻe ha peaukula ha kakai ne laka hake ʻi he toko 200 pea fakaʻauha mo ha ngaahi fale ne laungeau ʻi Donggala.
Ne toe tō foki ha peaukula ʻi he hihifo ʻo Donggala ʻi he 1996 ʻo mate ai ha toko hiva.
ʻOku hekeheka foki ʻa Indonesia ʻi he feituʻu fakatupunga mofuike ʻo e Pacific Ring of Fire pea ʻoku toutou tō maʻu pe mofuiké ai.
Ko e ngaahi mofuike lalahi ʻeni ne hoko ʻi he ngaahi taʻu ki muí:
2004: Ko ha mofuike lahi ʻi he matāfanga fakahihifo ʻo Indonesia ʻi he vahefonua Aceh ʻi he tokelau ʻo Sumatra ʻi he ʻaho 26 ʻo Tīsemá ʻa ia ne fakatupunga ha peaukula ne tō ʻi ha fonua ʻe 14, ʻo mate ai ha kakai ʻe toko 226,000 ʻi he matāfanga ʻo e ʻOseni ʻInitiá, ko e tokolahi ʻo e niʻihi ko iá ne ʻi Aceh.
2005: Ko e hohoko ʻo ha ngaahi mofuike mālohi ne tō ʻi he matāfanga fakahihifo ʻo Sumatra ʻi he konga ki mui ʻo Maʻasi pea mo e konga ki muʻa ʻo ʻEpelelí.
Ne mālōlō ha laungeau ʻi he Motu ko Nias, ʻi he ʻi tuʻa he matāfanga ʻo Sumatra.
2006: Ne tō ha mofuike ne mekinitute 6.8 ʻi he fakatonga ʻo Java, ko e motu tokolahi taha ia ʻo Indonesia, ne fakatupunga ʻe ha peaukula naʻá ne laiki ki he matāfanga fakatongá, ʻo tamateʻi ai ha kakai ne fakaofi hono tokolahí ki he toko 700.
2009: Ko ha mofuike ne mekinitute 7.6 naʻe tō ʻi he kolo ʻo Padang, ko e kolomuʻa ʻo e vahefonua ʻo Sumatra Hihifó
Ne mālōlō ha kakai ne laka hake ʻi he toko 1,100.
2010: Ne tō ha mofuike ne mekinitute 7.5 ʻi he taha ʻo e ngaahi motu ʻo Mentawai, ʻi tuʻa ʻi Sumatra, ʻo ne fakatupunga ha peaukula ne aʻu ki he mita ʻe 10 ʻa ia naʻá ne fakaʻauha ha ngaahi kolo lahi pea tamateʻi ha kakai ne aʻu ki he toko 300.
2016: Ne tō ha kiʻi mofuike ne lulu loloto ʻi lalo fonua ʻi he puleʻanga Pidie Jaya ʻi Aceh, ʻo fakatupunga ai ha ʻauha mo ha hohaʻa ʻi he kakai ne nau toe ʻi he fakatamaki ʻo e mofuike ʻo e 2004 pea moe peaukulá.
Ne ʻikai ha peaukula ne fakatupunga ʻi he taimi ko iá, ka ko naʻe laka hake ʻi he toko 100 ne mate ʻi he ngaahi fale ne holó.
2018: Ne tō ha mofuike lahi ʻi he motu folauʻeveʻeva ʻo Lombok, ʻo mate ai ha kakai ne laka hake ʻi he toko 500, ko e tokolahi ai ne ʻi he tafaʻaki fakatonga ʻo e motú.
Ne fakaʻauha ʻe he mofuiké ha ngaahi fale ʻe lauiafe pea tuku vakā ai mo ha kau folau ʻeveʻeva ne lauiafe.
Ne puke ʻa e lahi taha ʻo Sarah Palin ʻo tukuakiʻi ki ha Fakamamahi ʻi ʻApi
Kuo puke ʻa Track Palin, ko e foha lahi taha ʻo e kōvana ʻo Alaska pea mo e tokoni kanititeiti fakapalesiteni Sarah Palin, koeʻuhi ko hono tukuakiʻi ki ha hia tā.
Ne tukuakiʻi ʻa Palin taʻu 29 ʻo Wasilla ki ha mahaloʻi ʻo ha hia tā, kaunoa ʻi ha lipooti ʻo e fakamamahi ʻi ʻapí pea feinga ke taʻofi hono puke iá, fakatatau ki he lipooti ne tuku mai ʻi he ʻaho Tokonakí ʻe he Alaska State Troopers.
Fakatatau mo e lipooti meí he kau polisí, ʻi he taimi ne feinga ai ʻa hono kaungāmeʻa fefiné ke tā ki he polisí ke lipooti ʻa e hia ne tukuakiʻí, naʻá ne toʻo ʻa e telefoní mei he fefiné.
ʻOku kei tauhi maluʻi ʻa Palin ʻi he Fale Mat-Su Petrial pea ʻoku tauhi ʻi ha $500 pooni ʻikai maluʻi, ko e lipooti ia ʻa e KTUU.
Naʻe hā ʻi he fakamaauʻangá ʻi he ʻaho Tokonakí, ʻa ia naʻe fakahā ai" ʻoku ʻikai halaia, ko e moʻoni" ʻi he taimi ne ʻeke ai ki aí, ko e lipooti ia ʻa e netiueká.
Ne tautea Kalasi A ʻa Palin ki he fehalaaki siʻisiʻi, ʻo ʻuhinga ʻe lava pe ke tautea ngāue pōpula ʻo aʻu ki ha taʻu pea tautea paʻanga $250,000.
Ne toe tautea ʻi he Kalasi B ki he fehalaaki siʻisiʻí, ʻo tautea ʻaho ʻe taha ʻi pilīsone pea mo ha tautea paʻanga $2,000.
ʻOku ʻikai ko e ʻuluaki taimi ʻeni ne tautea hia ai ʻa Palin.
Ne tukuakiʻi ia ʻi Tīsema 2017 ki ha feinga fakalaveaʻi ʻene tamaí, Todd Palin.
Ne tā ʻene faʻeé, Sarah Palin, ki he kau polisí ke lipooti ʻa e ʻohofi ne tukuakiʻí.
Ko e keisí ʻoku lolotonga ʻi he Fakamaauʻanga Sōtia ʻo ʻAlasikaá.
ʻI Sanuali 2016 ne tukuakiʻi ai ia ki ha fakamamahi ʻi ʻapi, kaunoa ʻi hono lipooti ʻo e fakamamahi ʻi ʻapí, pea mo hono tauhi ʻo ha meʻa tau lolotonga ʻene huʻakavaʻiá ʻa ia ne kaunga ia mo e fakatamakí.
Ne tukuakiʻi ia ʻe hono kaumeʻa fefiné ki ha tuki naʻá ne fai ki hono matá.
Ne fakaangaʻi ʻe Sarah Pailin ʻa e kulupu sōtiá ʻi he 2016 hili ʻa hono fakafehokotaki ʻa e ʻulungaanga houtamaki hono fohá ki he PTSD ne fakatupunga mei heʻene ngāue fakakautau ʻi Iraq.
Mofuike Peaukula Indonesia: Mate Laungeau
Ne ʻi he kakai ʻe toko 384 ne mole ʻenau moʻuí hili ha tō ha mofuike ʻi Indonesia ʻi he motu ko Sulawesi he ʻaho Falaité.
Ne fakatupunga ʻe he mofuike mekinitute 7.5 ha peaukula pea kuo ne maumauʻi ha ngaahi ʻapi ʻe laungeau.
Kuo motuhia e ngaahi laine ʻuhilá mo e fetuʻutakí mo ha kau mate ʻoku ʻamanaki e toe tokolahi ange ʻi he ngaahi ʻaho ka hoko maí.
Ne tō ʻa e mofuiké ʻi tuʻa ʻi he vaheloto ʻo Sulawesi ʻa ia ʻoku ʻi he tokelauhahake ʻo e kolomuʻa ʻo Indonesia, ʻa Jakarta.
ʻOku ʻave takai ha ngaahi vitiō ʻi he mītia fakasōsialé ʻo fakahā ʻa e ngaahi mōmeniti ʻo e meʻa ne hokó.
Kuo fakataha mai ha kakai ʻe toko laungeau ki ha fakafiefia ʻi he matātahí ʻi he kolo ko Palú ne tō ʻa e peaukula ʻo ne maumauʻi ʻa e matāfangá.
ʻOku kei fakatotoloʻi ʻe he kau talatalaaki ʻa e fetuloló ha mate hāhāmolofia kau ki he taha ne mahaloʻi ki he ʻohofi fakatautoitoi ʻo NYC
ʻOku fakatotoloʻi ʻe he kau talatalaaki ʻa e fetulolo ʻi New York kau ki he tautea mate maʻa Sayfullo Saipov, ne mahaloʻi ki ai ʻa e ʻohofi fakakautau ne fai ʻi New York City ʻo mate ai ha kakai ʻe toko valu -- ko ha tautea hāhāmolofia ne teʻeki ke fakahoko ʻi he siteití ki ha hia fetulolo talu meí he 1953.
Kuo tukuakiʻi ʻa Saipov, taʻu 30 ki hono ngāueʻaki ha loli totongi meí he Home Depot ke fakahoko ʻaki ha ʻohofi ʻi ha halanga pasikala ʻi he Halalahi ʻo e West Side ʻi Lalo ʻi Manhattan, ʻo paeʻi ʻaki ʻa e kau lue laló mo e kau heka pasikala ne ʻi hono halá ʻi ʻOkatopa.
Koeʻuhi ke fakatonuhiaʻi ʻe hono tuʻutuʻuni maté, ʻe fiemaʻu ke fakamoʻoniʻi ʻe he kau talatalaakí naʻe fakahoko ʻe Saipov ʻi he "ʻiloʻilopau" ʻo ne tamateʻi ai ha niʻihi ʻe toko valu pea fakahoko "ʻiloʻilopau" ha fakalavea lahi ki he sino, ʻo fakatatau ki he fakahā ʻo e taumuʻá ke kumi ha tautea mate, ne faile ʻi he Vahenga Fakatonga ʻo New York.
Fakatoloua ʻo e ongo lau ko iá ne na ʻomi ha faingamālie tuʻutuʻuni mate, fakatatau ki he pepa fakamaauʻangá.
ʻI ha ngaahi uike hili ʻa e ʻohofí, ne tuku atu ʻe he kau sula ha lau ʻe 22 ne fakakau ha ngaahi tukuakiʻi ʻe valu ki he hia fakapō kau ki ai mo e fakamamahi, ne angamaheni hono ngāueʻaki ʻe he kau talatalaaki ʻa e fetuloló ke fokotuʻutuʻu ha ngaahi keisi fai hia, mo ha tukuakiʻi ki ha fakamamahi mo e fakaʻauha ʻo ha meʻalele.
ʻOku fiemaʻu ʻe he ʻohofí ha "palani lahi mo fakaʻaongaʻi ki muʻa," ne pehē ʻe he kau talatalaakí, ʻi hono fakamatalaʻi ʻa e ʻulungaanga ne fakahokoʻaki ʻe Saipov ne "fulikivanu, taʻeʻofa pea fakamasiva."
"Ne fakatupunga ʻe Sayfullo Habibullaevic Saipov ha fakalavea, fakatupu lavea, mo ha mole ki he ngaahi fāmili mo e kaungāmeʻa ʻo Diego Enrique Angelini, Nicholas Cleves, Ann-Laure Decadt, Darren Drake, Ariel Erlij, Hernan Ferruchi, Hernan Diego Mendoza, pea mo Alejandro Damian Pagnucco" ko ʻene ʻasi ia ʻi he fakahā ʻo e taumuʻá.
Ko e toko nima ʻo e kau mamahí ko ha kau folau ʻeveʻeva mei Argentina.
Kuo lava ha ta’u ‘e honogfulu talu ʻa e talatalaaki tautea mate fakamuimui taha ne fai ʻe he Vahe Fakatonga ʻo New York
Ko e fakaʻiloa, Khalid Barnes ne fakahalaʻiaʻi ki he fakapō ʻo e ongo tufaki faitoʻo kongatapu ka naʻe tauteaʻi ki he ngāue pōpula ki he mate ʻi Sepitema ʻo e 2009.
Ko e fakamuimui taha ʻo hono fakahoko ʻo ha tautea tāmate naʻe fakahoko ia ʻi he fetulolo ʻa New York ʻi he keisi ʻi he taʻu 1953 maʻa Julius mo Ethel Rosenberg, ko ha ongo meʻa mali ne fakapoongi hili hono fakahalaiaʻi ki naua ki hono faʻufaʻu ke fakahoko ha fakaasiasi ki he Soviet Union lolotonga ʻa e taʻu ʻe ua ki muʻa ʻi he Tau Momokó.
Ne tamateʻi fakatoloua ʻa e ongo Rosenbergs ʻi ha sea ʻuhila ʻi he ʻaho 19 ʻo Sune, 1953.
Ne fakahā ʻe Saipov, ko ha tangataʻi fonua ʻo Uzbekistan ha kiʻi loto mamahi siʻisiʻi ʻi he ngaahi ʻaho mo e māhina hili ʻa e ʻohofí, ʻo fakatatau mo e ngaahi fakamatala pepa meí he fakamaauʻangá.
Naʻá ne fakahā ki he kau fakatotoló naʻá ne ongoʻi lelei pē fekauʻaki mo e meʻa naʻá ne faí, ko e fakamatala ia ʻa e kau polisí.
Ne fakahā ʻe Sapov ki he kau maʻu mafaí ne ueʻi ia ke fakahoko ʻa e ʻohofi hili ʻene mamata ʻi he ngaahi vitiō ʻa e ISIS ʻi heʻene telefoní, ʻo fakatatau mo e tukuakiʻí.
Naá ne toe kole ke fakaʻaliʻali ʻa e fuka ʻo e ISIS ʻi hono loki falemahakí, pehē ʻe he kau polisí.
Kuo ne fakahā ʻoku ʻikai halaia ki he ngaahi lau ʻe 22 ʻo hono tukuakiʻí.
Ko e taha ʻo e kau maluʻi fetuloló ko David Patton, ʻa ia naʻá ne fakafofongaʻi ʻa Saipov, naʻá ne pehē ʻoku nau "matuʻaki lotomamahi" ʻi he tuʻutuʻuni ʻa e talatalaakí.
"ʻOku mau fakakaukau ko e tuʻutuʻuni ke fakahoko ʻa e tautea maté ʻo ʻikai ke tali ha kole ki ha moʻui ʻi pilīsone ʻo ʻikai lava ke tukuange te ne fakaloloa pe ʻe ia ʻa e faingataʻa ʻo e ngaahi meʻá ni ki he niʻihi kotoa pē ʻoku kaunga ki aí," pehē ʻe .
Ne kole ki muʻa ʻe he timi maluʻi ʻa Saipov ki he kau talatalaakí ke ʻoua te nau fakahoko ha tautea mate.
Pehē ʻe Tory MP ʻoku totonu ke fokotuʻu a NIGEL FARAGE ke ne tokangaʻi ʻa e ngaahi alea kau ki he Brexit
Ne tukupā ʻa Nigel Farage ke 'fetukutuku e kau tau ʻa e kakaí' he ʻahó ni lolotonga ha fakahāhāloto ʻi he konifelenisi ʻa Tory.
Ne pehē ʻe he taki mālōlō ʻa e Ukip ne fiemaʻu ke 'ongoʻi ʻa e kakahá' meí he kau fakafepaki ʻo e tupulaki ʻa ʻIulopé - ko ha taha ʻo e kau Mēmipa Fale Alea ʻa Theresa May naʻá ne fokotuʻu ʻoku totonu ke ne puleʻi ʻa e fealeapauʻaki mo e ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé.
Naʻe pehē ʻe he mēmipa falealea taʻe maʻu lakanga ʻi he puleʻangá ʻo e Faʻahi Konisevativí 'ne ʻosi mei ʻi tuʻa ' ʻa UK ʻi he taimí ni kapau naʻe Sekelitali Brexit ʻa Mr Farage.
Ka ko e pole ʻoku fekatulaki mo Mrs May ʻi hono fakatonutonu ʻa hono tuʻunga matuʻaki mavahevahé kuo fakailongaʻi ʻe he kaku poupou pro-Remain Tories ke kau ki ha fakahāhā makehe ʻo ʻikai poupouʻi ʻa Brexit ʻi he koló.
ʻOku faingataʻaʻia ʻa e palēmiá ke tauhi ʻene palani ki he Chequers (meʻaʻanga ʻo e palēmia Pilitānia) ʻi he lotolotonga ʻo e ʻohofi meí he tafaʻaki ʻa e kau Brexiteers (kau poupou ki he mavahe ʻa Pilitānia mei he ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé), Remainers (kau poupou ke nofo maʻu ʻa Pilitānia ʻi he ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé) pea mo e ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé.
Ne loto ʻa e ngaahi fonua poupoú te ne teke ki muʻa ʻaki haʻá ne feinga ke tauʻi ʻa e aleapau mo Brussel neongo ʻa e fakafetau - mo e fakamalohi ki he kau Euroseptics (niʻihi ʻoku nau fakafetau ki he fakaivia e malohi ʻo e ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé) pea mo e paati ʻa e Leipē ke fili ʻihe vahaʻa ʻo ʻene palaní pea mo e 'moveuveu'.
Ne tala ʻe Mr Bone ki he fakataha ʻo e Leave Means Leave (kulupu poupou ke mavahe ʻa Pilitānia meí he ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopē) ʻi Solihull ʻokú ne fiemaʻu ke 'liʻaki ʻa e Chequer (fokotuʻu ke nofo maʻu ʻa Pilitānia ʻi he ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé)'.
Naʻá ne fokotuʻu ʻa Mr Farage ne totonu ke hoko ko ha kaungā ngāue pea ʻoange ha fatongia ke alea mo Brussels.
'Kapau naʻá ne tokangaʻi, ne mei pehé ni kuo tau hū ki tuʻa,' ko ʻene leá ia.
To e tānaki ʻatu ʻe he Mēmipa Fale Alea ʻa Wellingborough: 'Te u tuʻu hake maʻá Brexit ka ʻoku fiemaʻu ke tau tuku ki tuʻa ʻa e Fokotuʻu ke nofo ʻa Pilitānia ʻi he ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé.'
Fokotuʻu ʻene kau fakafepakí ki he ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé, naʻá ne pehē: 'Ne ʻikai ke tau tau ʻi he ngaahi tau lahi ʻa māmaní ke tau fakaongoongo ki ha to e pule.
ʻOku fiemaʻu ke tau faʻu ʻetau lao pē ʻa tautolu ʻi he fonua ʻo kiatutolú.'
Naʻe tukuange ʻe Mr Bone ʻa e ngaahi fokotuʻu ki he liliu ki he fakakaukau ʻa e kakaí talu meí he fili ʻo e 2016: 'Ko e fakakaukau ʻo pehē kuo liliu ʻa e fakakaukau ʻo e kakai ʻo Pilitāniá pea ʻoku nau loto ke nofoí ʻoku matuʻaki loi ia.'
Ne toe ʻi he laká foki ʻa Tory Brexiteer Andrea Jenkyns ʻo ne fakahā ki he kau faiongoongó : 'ʻOku ou pehē: Palēmia, fanongo ki he kakaí.
'ʻOku ʻikai manakoa ʻa e Chequers ʻi he kakaí katoa, ʻe ʻikai ke fili ʻa e kau Fakafepakí ki ai, ʻoku ʻikai manakoa ia ʻi heʻemau paatí pea mo ʻemau kau poupoú ʻa ia ʻoku nau poupou ʻi he halá pea mo feinga ke fili kiimautolú.
Kātaki ʻo liʻaki ʻa e Fokotuʻu ke kei nofo ʻa Pilitānia ʻi he ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé pea mou feinga ke fanongo.'
ʻI ha pōpoaki fakahangatonu kia Mrs May, naʻá ne tānaki atu: 'ʻOku tauhi ʻe he kau Palēmiá ʻenau ngāué ʻi he taimi ʻoku nau tauhi ai ʻenau palōmesí.'
Ne fakahā ʻe Mr Farage ki he fakatahá ʻoku totonu ke ngaahi ʻa e kau tangata politikalé ke nau 'ongoʻi ʻa e velá' ʻo kapau te nau kamata ke liʻaki ʻa e tuʻutuʻuni ne fakahoko ʻi he paloti ʻo e 2016.
'Ko ha meʻa ʻeni kau ki he falala ʻi hotau vahaʻá - ʻa e kakaí - pea mo e faʻahinga ʻi he politikí,' naʻá ne lea ʻaki ia.
'ʻOku nau feinga ke lavakiʻi ʻa Brexit pea ʻoku tau ʻi heni he ʻahó ni ke tala kia kinautolu 'ʻe ʻikai ke mau tukuange kimoutolu ke mou fakahoko ia.'
ʻI ha pōpoaki ki he matanga vilitakí naʻá ne pehē: 'ʻOku ou fiemaʻu kimoutolu ke mou ngaahi homou kau politikí, ʻa ia ʻoku nauʻ i he tuliki ʻo hono lavakiʻi ʻa Brexit, ongoʻi ʻa e vevela.
'ʻOku mau fetukutuku ʻa e kau sotia kakai ʻo e fonuá ni ʻa ia ʻoku nau poupouʻi e ikuna ʻa e Brexit pea ʻe ʻikai mālōlō kae ʻoleva ke tau hoko ʻo tauʻatāina, puleʻi pē hotau puleʻangá, polepole ʻi Pilitānia.'
ʻI he taimi tatau, ne laka takai ʻa e kau Remainers (poupou ke nofo pē ʻa Pilitānia ʻi he ʻIunioni ʻa ʻIulopé) ki muʻa pea fakahoko ʻenau fakataha houa ua ʻi he lotolotonga ʻo e koló.
Ne taʻataʻalo ʻa kiʻi kau poupoú ʻaki ha ngaahi fakaʻilonga mo e tā ʻo Tories ʻIkai Poupouʻi Brexit hili ʻa hono fokottuʻu ʻa e kulupú ʻi he fakaʻosinga uiké.
Ne fakaangaʻi ʻe he kaungā mateakiʻi Leipa ko Lord Adonis ʻa e Konisevativí ki heʻenau palopalema fakaēmalú ne nau fepaki mo ia ʻi ha polokalama ʻo ʻenau faʻahi ʻi he fakaava ʻo e konifelenisí.
'Ko e kakai eni ‘oku nau talamai te nau lava pē ʻo maʻu ʻa e IT system (Sisitemi Fakamatala Tekinolosiá) ke maau pea mo e tekinolosia kotoa maʻá e totongi sēvesi (plus plus) ʻa Kānatá, ki he kauʻāfonua faingofuá, ki he fefakatauʻaki taʻetotongi ʻo ʻikai ha kauʻāfonua ʻi Ireland,' naʻá ne tānaki atu.
'Ko e fakaoli kotoa ia.
ʻOku ʻikai ha meʻa ʻe lelei ange ʻi he Brexit,' naʻá ne tānaki atu.
Palani ʻa Warren ke 'sio lahi' ki he lele fili palesiteni
Puleʻanga ʻAmeliká Pehe ʻe Senatoa Elizabeth te ne fakahoko ha "sio lahi kie lele fili palesteni" hili ʻa e fili ʻi Nōvemá.
Ne lipooti ʻe he Boston Globe ne talanoa ʻa e Temokalati ʻo Massachusetts kau ki hono kahaʻú lolotonga ha fakataha ʻi Masasute Hihifo ʻi he Tokonakí.
Ko Warren, ko ha taha fakaanga ʻo Palesiteni Donald Trump, ʻoku lele ki he to e fili ʻi Nōvemá pehē ki he Fakafofonga siteiti ko Geoff Diehl, ʻa ia naʻe tokoni sea ki he kemipeini ʻa Massachusett maʻa Trump ʻi he 2016.
Kuo ʻi he lotolotonga ʻo e fakamahamahalo te ne poleʻi ʻa Trump ʻi he 2020.
Ko e polokalama ʻi he hoʻatā Tokonakí ʻi Holyoke ko ʻene fakataha fika 36 ia mo e fakafofonga vahenga ʻo ngāueʻaki ʻa e fale fakapuleʻangá talu e ngāue ʻa Trump ʻi hono tuʻungá.
Ne fehuʻi ʻe ha tokotaha ne maʻu fakataha pe ʻoku palani ke lele ki he fili palesitení.
Ne tali ʻa Warren ki ai "Kuo taimi ki he houʻeiki fafiné ke nau ō ki Uasingatoni ʻo fakaleleiʻi hotau puleʻanga maumaú pea ʻoku kau ki ai ha fefine ke ʻi he tumutumú."
Puke ne fai he mate ʻi ha fana ʻa Sims ʻi LSU
Ne fakahā ʻe he kau polisi ʻi Baton Rouge, La., ʻihe Tokonakí ʻa hono puke ha taha ʻo mahaloʻi ki ha fana ʻo mate ha tokotaha vaʻinga pasiketipolo ʻi LSU ko Wayde Sims ʻi he ʻaho Falaité.
Ne fakahā ʻe he Vaʻa Polisi ʻa Baton Rouge ne fai hono puke ʻo Dyteon Simpson taʻu 20 ʻi he 11 pongipongi. ʻi ha fakataha ʻa e kau faiongoongo ET.
Kuo nau tukuange mai ha vitiō ʻo e fana ʻi he Falaité, mo e kole ki ha tokoni ki hono ʻiloʻi ʻo e tangata ʻi he vitioó.
Ne fanaʻi ʻo mate ʻa Sims taʻu 20 ʻo ofi ki he ʻapiako ʻUnivēsiti Fakahahaké ʻi he pongipongi Falaité.
"Ne faingataʻaʻia ʻa Wayde Sims ʻi ha fana ʻi hono ʻulú pea ne iku mālōlō ai," ko e fakamatala ia ʻa e pule polisi ko Murphy J. Paul ki he ongoongó ʻi he Tokonakí, ko e ngaahi sipoti 247.
Ne manga atu ʻa Wayde ke maluʻi hono kaungāmeʻá pea ne fanaʻi ai ia ʻe Simpson.
Ne fakaʻekeʻeke ʻa Simpson pea ne fakahā ʻi heʻene ʻasí, naʻá ne tauhi ha meʻatau, pea fakahā ʻa ʻene fanaʻi ʻa Wayde Sims.
Ne puke ʻa Simpson ʻo ʻikai ha palopalema pea ne ʻave ai pē ʻo fakahū maluʻi ʻi he ʻApi Polisi ʻi East Baton Rouge.
Ko ha tokotaha fute 6.6 ʻokú ne hono taʻu hono ua he akó, naʻá ne tupu hake pē ʻi Baton Rouge, ne vaʻinga ʻa Sims ʻi ha tau ʻe 32 ʻo kamataʻaki ʻa e 10 ʻi he faʻahitaʻu kuoʻosí ʻi ha ʻavalisi ko e miniti ʻe 17.4 poini ʻe 5.6 pea mo ha fakahū 2.9 ʻi he vaʻinga kotoa.
Pale Lahi ʻa Lūsiá: Fakaofi mai ʻa Lewis Hamilton ki he hingoa ʻo māmaní hili ʻa e fiemaʻu ʻa e timí ke ne maʻu ʻa e ikuna ʻi he tau mo Sebastian Vettel
Ne hā mahino meí he mōmeniti ne laka mo feʻunga ai ʻa Valtteri Bottas ki muʻa ʻia Lewis Hamilton he ʻaho Tokonakí ne" fekau ʻe he timi ʻa Mercedes ke vaʻingaʻi ʻa e konga lahi ʻi he lová.
Meí he pamú, ne fakahoko ʻe Bottas ha kamataʻanga lelei pea meimei tautau ʻa Hamilton ʻi tuʻa ke mōmoa ʻi heʻene maluʻi hono tuʻungá ʻi he fuofua afe ʻe uá pea mo fakaafeʻi ʻa Vettel ke ʻohofi hono kaungā timí.
Ne ʻuluaki lele atu ʻa Vettel ki he luó pea mavahe ʻa Hamilton ke lele atu ki he ngaahi ka lová ʻi he hiku ʻo e kulupú, ko ha meʻa ne tonu ke fuʻu fakapapauʻi.
Ne taki atu ʻa e Mercedes ʻi ha lele fakalaka pea muimui atu ʻi mui ʻia Vettel ka ne taki atu ʻa Hamilton hili haʻana lele matamata tatau ne ʻilo atu ai ʻa e fakaʻuli ʻo e Ferrari ʻoku veiveiua ke mahave ʻa e tafaʻaki ki loto ne ʻikai ha toe fakaʻatungia ai hili ha ngaʻunu tāpolo ke maluʻi ʻa e tuliki fika tolú.
Ne kamata atu ʻa Max Verstappen meí he fakaʻosinga ʻo e ʻotú pea naʻe ʻi he fika fitu ʻi he fakaʻosinga ʻo e ʻuluaki takaí ʻi hono taʻu 21.
Naʻá ne taki ʻi he taimi lahi ʻo e lová ʻi heʻene puke atu ki heʻene vaʻé ke fakapapauʻi ha fakaʻosinga vave pea mo fakalaka ʻia Kimi Raikkonen ne ʻi he fika faá.
Ne fakaʻau ke haʻu ki he ngaahi luó ʻi he fakalata tuʻo 44 ka naʻe ʻikai ke lava ke hiki ʻene toó ʻi he toenga ʻo e fakalaka fika valú ʻi he lele ʻa Raikkonen ʻi heʻene fika faá.
Ko ha ʻaho faingataʻa koeʻuhi ne fakahoko ʻe Valtteri ha feinga lelei ʻi he fakaʻosinga uiké kotoa pea ne hoko ia ko ha tangata lelei.
Ne fakahoko ʻe he ongo timí ha ngāue fakaholomamata ke maʻu ai ha taha ua," ko e lau ia ʻa Hamilton.
Ko ha Fakafotunga Matuʻaki Kovi Moʻoni
Ne fakaangaʻi ʻe Palesiteni Donald Trump ʻa Senatoa Dianne Feinstein ʻi ha fakataha ʻi he ʻaho Tokonakí ʻi heʻene fakapapauʻi ne ʻikai ke ne tuku ki tuʻa ʻa e tohi meí a Christine Blasey Ford ʻo tukuakiʻi ʻa e taha teu fili ko Brett Kavanaugh ki he Fakamaauʻanga Lahí ki ha ʻohofi fakasekisuale.
ʻI haʻane lea ʻi he fakataha ne fai ʻi West Virginia, naʻe ʻikai ke lea fakahangatonu ko e fakamoʻoni ne fai ʻe Ford ʻi muʻa ʻi he Komiti Fakamaau Senatoa, makehe mei heʻene fakamatala ko e meʻa ia ne hoko ʻi he Senatoa ne fakahā ko e kakai ne nau "angakovi mo anga palakū mo taʻemoʻoni."
"Ko e meʻa ʻe taha ne mei hoko pea mo e meʻa fakaʻofoʻofa ne hoko ʻi he ngaahi ʻaho fakaʻosi heʻene ʻi he Senatoá, ʻi hoʻo sio ki he ʻitá, ʻi hoʻo sio ki he kakai ʻoku fakapoʻulí pea anga palakū pea taʻemoʻoní," naʻá ne pehē.
"ʻI hoʻo sio ki he ngaahi meʻa ʻoku tuku maí pea tuku ki tuʻá pea nau pehē "ʻoi, ne ʻikai ke u fai ia.
Naʻe ʻikai ke u fai ia."
Manatuʻí?
Dianne Feinstein, naʻá ke mama ia ki tuʻá?
Manatuʻi ʻene talí... naʻá ke tuku ki tuʻu ʻa e tohi fakamatalá - "ʻoi, ʻoi, ko e hā?
Fakapō.
Naʻe ʻikai ke u tuku ia ki tuʻa."
Ko ia, tali miniti pē taha.
Ne mau tuku ki tuʻa...ʻIkai, ne ʻikai ke mau tuku ki tuʻa," naʻá ne tānaki atu, ki loto ko ha ongo ia ʻa e senatoá.
Ne ʻave ʻa e tohi kia Feinstein ʻo fakaikiiki ʻa e tukuakiʻi kia Kavanaugh ʻaki ʻe Ford ʻi Siulai, pea naʻe tuku ki tuʻa ʻi he konga ki muʻa ʻo Sepitemá - ka naʻe fakaʻikaiʻi ʻe Feinstein naʻá ne tuku ki tuʻa mei hono ʻofisí.
"Ne ʻikai ke u toitoi Toketā. Ngaahi tukuakiʻi ʻo Ford" Ne tala ʻe Feinstein ki he kōmití, ko e lipooti ia ʻa e The Hill.
"Naʻá ne ʻeke mai ke puke ʻo ʻikai fakahāhā holo pea ne u tauhi iaʻo ʻikai fakahāhā holo ʻo fakatatau mo ʻene kolé."
Ka naʻe ʻikai hā ʻene fakaʻikai ke mahinoʻi ʻe he palesitení, ʻa ia naʻe fakamatala ʻi he lolotonga ʻo e fakataha ʻi he pō Tokonakí: "ʻOku ou talaatu, ko ha fakafotunga matuʻaki kovi moʻoni
Mahalo ne ʻikai, ka ko e fakafotunga sino kovi moʻoni ia kuó u sio aí."
ʻI heʻene hokohoko ʻene maluʻi taha ke fili ki he Fakamaauʻanga Lahí, ʻa ia kuo tukakiʻi ki ha ʻulungaanga fakafeʻauaki ʻe ha kakai fefine ʻe toko tolu, ne fokotuʻu ʻe he palesitení ne ngāueʻaki ʻe he kau Temokālatí ʻa e tukuakiʻí ki heʻenau fiemaʻú.
"ʻOku nau fakapapauʻi ke fakafoki ʻa e mālohí ʻaki ha meʻa pē ʻe fiemaʻu.
ʻOke sio ki he angakoví, ko e palakuú, ʻoku ʻikai ke nau tokanga ko hai ʻe mamahí, ko hai te nau tāmolo ai ke maʻu ʻa e mālohí pea mo e pulé," ko e lipooti ia ʻe Mediaite ʻa e palesitení.
Liiki ʻĒlití: Stars ʻo Dunedee 5-3 moe Giants ʻo Belfast
Ne taaʻi ʻe Patrick Dwyer ha kai ʻe ua maʻá e Giants ʻi heʻene tau mo eDundee
Ne huhuʻi ʻe Dundee Stars ki he foʻi ʻi he Liiki ʻĒliti ʻo e ʻaho Falaité ʻi he Giants ʻo Belfast ʻaki ʻa e ikunga ko e 5-3 ʻi Dundee ʻi he Tokonakí.
Ne maʻu ʻe he Giants ha kolo ʻe ua ʻo taki atu ki he tā meí a Patrick Dwyer mo Francis Beauvillier.
Ne ʻomi ʻe Mike Sullivan pea mo Jordan Cownie ʻa e vaʻinga ki he tafaʻaki ʻo e timi talitalí ki muʻa pea fakafoki ʻe Dwyer ʻa e takí ki he Giants.
Ne ʻomi ʻe Francos Bouchard ha kai tatau maʻá e Dundee ki muʻa pea kolo ʻe ua ʻa Lukas Lundvald Nieldsen ʻo ne maluʻi ai ikuná.
Ko ha ikuna ia ʻe tolu ʻi he Liiki ʻĒliti ʻo e faʻahitaʻu vaʻingá maʻá e kau tangata ʻa Adam Keefe, ʻa ia ne nau haʻu mei mui ke taaʻi ʻa e Dundee ʻi ha kai ko e 2-1 ʻi Belfast ʻi he pō Falaité.
Ko e fetaulaki tuʻu fā ia ʻa e ongo faʻahí ʻi he faʻahitaʻú, mo e Giants ne nau ikuna ʻa e ngaahi tau ʻe tolu ki muʻá.
Ne haʻu ʻa e ʻoupeni ʻa e Dwyer ʻi he miniti ʻe faá ʻi he 3:35 mei ha tokoni ʻa Kendall McFaull, peá mo David Rutherford naʻá ne fakahoko ha tokoni ʻi hono tāpoloʻi mai ʻe he Beauvillier ʻa e taki ʻi he miniti ʻe fa mei ai.
ʻI ha kamataʻanga moʻumoʻua, ne ʻomi ai ʻe Sullivan ʻa e tafaʻaki talitalí ki loto ki he vaʻingá ʻi he 13:10 ki muʻa pea hoko ʻa Matta Marquardt ko he tokoni ki hono fakapalanisi (equaliser) ʻe Crownie ʻi he 15:16.
Ne fakapapauʻi ʻe Dwyer ʻoku taki ʻa e Giants ki he mālōlō ʻuluakí ʻi heʻene taaʻi ʻa e kai hono ua ʻo e poó ʻi he fakaʻosinga ʻo e ʻuluaki tuʻu.
Ko e faʻu kulupu ʻa e timi talitalí pea toe fokotuʻu kinautolu ʻe Bouchard ʻi he teemi levoló ʻaki ha vaʻinga malohi ʻo kai ʻi he 27:37.
Ne fakataha ʻe Cownie mo Charles Corocoran ke tokonia ʻa Nielsen ke ʻave ʻa e takí ki he Dundee ʻi he fuofua taimí ʻi he tau ne tomui ʻi he tuʻu hono uá pea naʻá ne fakapapauʻi ke mālohi mo ʻene timí ʻi he lolotonga ʻo e toʻu fainoló.
Kuo ulungia ʻa e Giants ʻi ha tau ʻe fā ʻo e ʻenau ngaahi tau ʻe nima kuo hilí, ʻoku nau ʻi honau malaʻé kia Milton Keynes ʻi heʻenau tau hoko ʻi he Falaité.
Mālōlō ha Tangata Puleʻi ʻo e Fepunaʻaki ʻi he ʻEá ke Fakapapauʻi ʻoku Hola ʻa e Laungeau ne ʻI he Vakapuná
Ne fakahikihikiʻi ha helo ka ko ha tangata ʻokú ne puleʻi ʻa e fepunaʻaki ʻi he ʻeá ʻi heʻene pekia lolotonga ʻene feinga ke tō lelei mo malu ha vakapuna ne ʻi ai ha kau pasese ʻe laungeau.
Ne laka hake ʻi ha kakai ʻe toko 800 ne nau mālōlō pea ne tokolahi ne mole hili ha mofuike lahi naʻe tō ʻi he motu ʻo Sulawesi ʻi he Falaité, ʻo ne fakatupunga ai ha peaukula.
Ne hoko atu ha ngaahi lulu mālohi ʻa ia ne hokohoko atu ʻene uesia ʻa e ʻēliá pea mo e niʻihi tokolahi ne taʻomia ʻi he veve ʻi he kolo ko Palú.
Ka neongo ne hola hono ngaahi kaungā ngāué koeʻuhi ko ʻenau moʻuí, ne fakafisinga ʻe Anthonius Gunawan Agung taʻu 21 ke mavahe mei heʻene ngāué ʻi he taimi ne lulu lahi ai ʻa e taua pulé (control) ʻi he Malaʻevakapuna Palu ʻi Mutiara Sis Al.
Naʻá ne nofo maʻu ke fakapapauʻi ne lava ʻa e Vakapuna Batik Air Flight 6321, ke puna lelei ʻa ia ne lolotonga ʻi he halanga vakapuná ʻi he taimi ko ia.
Ne ʻosi ia peá ne puna ki lalo meí he tauá ʻi heʻene fakakaukau ne holo.
Naʻá ne mate ki mui ʻi he falemahakí.
Ne pehē ʻe he fakafofonga maʻá e Fefolauʻaki Vakapuna ʻa Indonesia, Yohannes Sirait, ko e tuʻutuʻuní ne mei fakahaofi ha moʻui ʻe laungeau, ko e lipooti ia ʻa e Ongoongo ABC ʻa Australia.
Ne mau teuteuʻi ha helekopeta mei Balikpapn ʻi Kalimantan ke ʻave ia ki ha falemahaki lahi ʻi ha loto ʻe taha.
Ko e meʻa fakamamahí ne siʻi hiki ia he pongipongí ni ki muʻa pea aʻu atu e helekopetá ki Palú.
"ʻOku ongo ki homau lotó ke fanongo ki he meʻá ni," naʻá ne tānaki atu.
ʻI he taimi tatau, ʻoku manavahē ʻa e kau takí ki he hiki ʻa e fika ʻo e kau maté naʻa ala ʻo aʻu ki he lauafe ne pehē ʻehe kautaha tokangaekina ʻo e fakatamakí ʻoku fakangatangata ʻa e hū ki he ngaahi kolo ʻo Donggala, Sigi pea mo Boutong.
"Ko e tokolahi ʻo e kau maté ʻoku fakautuutu ki ʻolunga lolotonga ʻoku kei tanu ha ngaahi sino ʻi lalo ʻi he ngaahi meʻa ne holó pea ʻi ai ha tokolahi ne teʻeki ke lava ke aʻu kia nautolu," ko e fakamatala ia ʻa e fakafofonga ʻo e kautahá Sutopo Purwo Nugroho.
Ne aʻu ʻa e ngaahi peaú ki he mita ʻe onó kuó ne maumauʻi ʻa Palu ʻa ia ʻe fai ai ha tanu tokolahi ʻi he ʻaho Sāpaté.
ʻOku lolotonga fetuku mai ʻe he vakapuna fakakautaú mo e fakalotofonuá ʻa e ngaahi tokoní mo e fiemaʻú.
Ne fakahā ʻe Risa Kusuma, ko ha faʻē taʻu 35 ki he Ongoongo ʻa e Sky: "ʻI he miniti kotoa ne tau mai ai ʻa e meʻalele fakahaofimoʻuí (ambulance) mo ha ngaahi sino.
ʻOku siʻisiʻi mo e vaí.
ʻOku hae mo fakaʻauha ʻa e ngaahi falekoloa iikí ʻi he feituʻu kotoa pē."
Ne fakahā ʻe Jan Gelfand ko e taki ʻo e Kolosi Kula Fakatuʻapuleʻanga ʻa Indonesia ki he CNN: "ʻOku fakavave ʻa e Kolosi Kula ʻa Indonesia ke tokoniʻi ʻa e niʻihi ne kei moʻuí ka ʻoku ʻikai ke mau ʻilo ko e hā te nau maʻu aí.
"Kuo ʻosi hoko pē ʻeni ia ko ha fakatamaki, ka ʻoku malava pē ke toe kovi ange."
Kuo tuʻuta ʻa e Palesiteni ʻo Indonesia ʻi Palu ʻi he ʻaho Sāpaté pea tala ki he kau sōtia ʻo e fonuá: "ʻOku ou kole kia kimoutolu kotoa ke mou ngāue ʻaho mo e pō ke fakakakato ʻa e fiemaʻu kotoa ʻoku kaunga ki he fetukutukú.
ʻOkú ke mateuteu?" ne lipooti ʻe he CNN.
Ne tō ha mofuike ʻi Indonesia ʻi he kamataʻanga ʻo e taʻu ní ʻi Lombok ʻa ia ne pekia ai ha toko 550.
Pā e Vakapuna Micronesia: Pehē ʻe he Air Niugini ʻoku mole ha tangata hili e pā e vakapuná ʻi he anó
Ne fakapuna ʻe he kautaha vakapuná ha vakapuna ne pā ʻi he ano Pacific ʻi Micronesia ne pehē ne pulia ha tangata, hili ʻenau tuku mai ʻi he konga ki muʻá ʻo pehē ne lava hono fetukutuku lelei ʻa e kau pasese mo e kau ngāue vakapuna ʻe 47 meí he vakapuna ne ngotó.
Ne tuku mai ha fakamatala ʻa e Air Niugini ʻo pehē ʻi he hoʻatā Sāpaté ne faingatāmaki ke tokanga ki he kau pasese tangatá.
Ne pehē ʻe he kautaha vakapuná ne ngāue mo e kau maʻu mafai ʻo e fonuá, falemahakí, pea mo e kau fakatotoló ke feinga ke kumi ʻa e tangatá.
Ne ʻikai vave ʻa e tali ʻa e kautaha vakapuná he kole ki ha toe fakamatala fakaikiikí fekauʻaki mo e pasesé, ʻo hangē ko hono taʻú pe matakalí.
Ko e ngaahi vaka tahi ʻo e feituʻú ne kaufakiʻi ʻa e kau pasese kehé mo e kau kauvaká hili ʻa e tau ʻa e vakapuná ki he vaí lolotonga ʻene feinga ke fakatōtō ki he malaʻe vakapuna ʻo e motu Chuuk.
Ne pehē ʻe he kau ʻofisa maʻolungá ne ʻave ha kakai ʻe toko fitu ki he falemahakí he ʻaho Falaité.
Ne pehē ʻe he kautaha vakapuná ne kei toe ha kau pasese ʻe ono ʻi he falemahakí ʻi he ʻaho Tokonakí, pea ʻoku nau ʻi ha tuʻunga fakafiemālie kotoa pē.
ʻOku teʻeki mahino ʻa e tupunga ʻo e pā pea mo e hokohoko ʻo e meʻa ne hokó.
Ko e kautaha vakapuná pea mo e Puleʻanga ʻAmeliká Ne fakatou pehē ʻe he Tautahí ne tuʻuta ʻa e vakapuná ʻi he anó ʻi he nounou ʻa e halanga vakapuná.
Ne fakakaukau ha niʻihi ʻo e kau fakamoʻoní ne fakalaka ʻa e vakapuná ʻi he leleʻanga vakapuná.
Ne pehē ʻe ha pasese ʻAmelika ko Bill Jaynes ne ʻalu hifo maʻulalo ʻa e vakapuná.
"Ko ha meʻa matuʻaki lelei ia" ne pehē ʻe Jaynes.
Ne pehē ʻe Jaynes ko ia mo e toengá ne nau lava ʻo ngāue holo ʻi ha vai ne aʻu hake ki honau kongalotó ʻo aʻu ki he hūʻanga fakavavevave ki tuʻa ʻo e vakapuná.
Naʻá ne pehē ne hohaʻa ʻa e kau ngāue vakapuná mo nau kaikaila, pea ko ia naʻe lavea siʻisiʻi ai hono ʻulú.
Ko e Puleʻanga ʻAmeliká Ne pehē ʻe he Tautahí ne ngāue ʻa e kau kauvaká ʻo ofi ki ha uafu ne kei ngaahi pea mo tokoni ke kaufaki ʻo ngāueʻaki ha vaka leta ke feʻaveʻaki e kakaí ki he matāfangá ki muʻa pea ngoto hifo ʻa e vakapuná ʻi ha mita ʻe 30 (100 loloto) ʻo e vaí.
Ne fakahā ʻe ha fakamatala meí he Kulupu Fengāueʻaki Malu Vakapuná ha kakai ʻe toko 111 ne nau mate ʻi he pā ʻo ha vaka ne lēsisita ʻi Papua Niu Kini ʻi he taʻu ʻe uanoa ka naʻe ʻikai fakakau ʻa e Air Niugini.
Ne fakahā ʻe ha taha ʻanalaiso ha taimi ʻo ha fefine poʻuli ne tutu moʻui
Ne mālōlō ʻa hono talatalaakiʻi ʻa ʻene keisí ʻi he ʻaho Tokonakí ʻi hono toe hopoʻi ha tangata naʻe tukuakiʻi ki hono tutu moʻui ha fefine Misisipi ʻi he 2014 .
Puleʻanga ʻAmeliká Ne fakamoʻoni ʻa Paul Rowlett ʻi ha ngaahi houa ko ha mataotao ʻi he malaʻe ʻo e ʻanalaiso poto ʻi he Vaʻa ʻo e Fakamaau Totonu ʻAnalaisó.
Naʻá ne fakamatala ki he kau sula ki he founga naʻá ne ngāueʻaki ʻa e meʻa hiki ʻi he telefoní ke fakatahaʻi ʻaki ʻa e ngaahi ngaʻunu ʻa e fakaʻiloa taʻu 29 ko Quinton Tellis pea ko e mamahi taʻu 19, Jessica Chambers ʻi he pō naʻa mate aí.
Ne pehē ʻe Rowlett naʻá ne maʻu ha fakamatala ʻo ha feituʻu meí ha ngaahi telefoni toʻotoʻo ne fakahā ai naʻe fakataha ʻa Tellis mo Chambers ʻi he efiafi ne mālōlō aí, ʻo ʻikai fenāpasi ia mo ʻene fakamatala ki muʻá, ko e lipooti ia ʻa e The Clarion Ledger .
ʻI he hā ʻa e fakamatalá ʻi heʻene telefoni toʻotoʻó ne ʻia Chambers lolotonga ʻa e taimi naʻá ne pehē ne ʻi hano kaungāmeʻa Michael Sanford, ne ʻalu ai ʻa e kau polisí ʻo talanoa mo Sanford.
Ne tuʻu ʻa Sanford ki he tuʻungá ʻi he Tokonakí pea ne fakamoʻoni ne ʻikai ke ne ʻi kolo ʻi he ʻaho ko iá.
ʻI he taimi ne ʻeke ai ʻe he kau talatalaakí pe naʻe fakahā ʻe Tellis ʻa e moʻoní ʻi heʻene pehē ne ʻi he loli ʻa Sanford ʻi he pō ko iá, naʻe pehē ʻe Sanford naʻá ne "loi, koeʻuhi ne ʻi Nashville ʻeku lolí."
Ko ha toe talanoa ne ʻikai hokohoko lelei ʻa e tala ʻe Tellis naʻá ne ʻilo pē ʻa Chambers ʻi ha uike pē ʻe ua ʻi he taimi ne mate aí.
Ne fakahā ʻe he lekooti ʻo e telefoni toʻotoʻó ne toki maheni pē ʻi ha uike ʻe taha.
Naʻe pehē ʻe Rowlett ne ʻiai ha ngaahi taimi hili ʻa e mate ʻa Chambers, ne tamateʻi ai ʻe Tellis ʻa e ngaahi tohi telefoni ʻa Chambers, ngaahi tā telefoní mo e ngaahi fakamatala fetuʻutakí mei heʻene telefoní.
"Naʻá ne tamateʻi ʻene moʻuí mei heʻene telefoní," ne pehē ʻe Hale.
Ko e maluʻi ʻoku fokotuʻu ke kamata ʻene fakakikihi fakaʻosí ʻi he Sāpaté.
Ne pehē ʻe he fakamaaú ʻokú ne ʻamanaki ke ʻave ʻa e hopo ki he kau sulá ʻi he konga ki mui ʻo e ʻaho ko iá.
Ko e High Breed : Koe hā ʻa e hip hop ʻilo lelei?
ʻOku fiemaʻu ʻe he kau tisikou hip hop toko tolú ke nau poleʻi ʻa e fakakaukau kovi ʻo e faʻahinga ʻaki ʻa hono fakafonu ʻenau hivá ʻaki ha ngaahi pōpoaki lelei.
Ne poupouʻi ʻe he High Breed, mei Bristol ʻa e mavahe ʻa e hip hop ʻo mamaʻo mei hono kamataʻangá ʻa ia ko e pōpoaki fakapolitikale pea mo hono taukaveʻi ʻo e ngaahi palopalea fakasōsialé.
ʻOku nau fiemaʻu ke nau foki ki he uhó pea fakaivia ʻa e toe manakoa ʻa e hiva hip hop.
Ko e kau hiva hangē ko e The Fugees pea mo e Common kuo nau mamata ki he fakaakeake kimuí ni ʻi Pilitānia ʻo fakafou ʻi he kau hiva ʻo hangē ko Akala pea mo Lowkey.
Ko ha toe tokotaha ʻuliʻuli ʻe taha?!
Ne suuʻi ʻe ha neni NY ha ongomātuʻa ne na fana ʻi he ʻosi ha fetohiʻaki telefoni "laulanu"
ʻOku fakaʻilo ʻe ha neni mei New York ha ongomātuʻa ki hano tuli ia ʻi ha laulanu hili hano maʻu ha fetohiʻaki telefoni ne ʻave halaʻi meí ha faʻē naʻá ne hanu ʻo pehē ko ia ko "ha toe tokotaha ʻuliʻuli."
Ne fakahalaʻi ʻe he ongo meʻá ʻokú na laulanu, ʻo tala ko e fakaʻiló ne fai ʻi he "fakamanamana."
Ne fakahā ʻe Lynsey Palsco-Flaxman, ko ha faʻē ʻo ha fanau ʻe tokoua, ʻa ʻene loto mamahi ʻi heʻene ʻilo ko e tokotaha tokangaēkina e fanau foʻou ko Giselle Maurice, ko e tokotaha ʻuliʻuli ʻi heʻene aʻu atu ki heʻene fuofua ʻaho he ngāue ʻi he 2016.
"ʻIIIIIKKKKKKKAAAAAAAIIII KO E TOE ʻULIʻULI E ʻE TAHA," ko e tohi ia ʻa Mrs Plasco-Flaxman ʻi he telefoní ki hono husepānití.
Kaikehe, ne ʻikai ke ʻave ia ʻe ia ki hono husepānití ka ne ʻave ʻe ia kia Ms. Maurice, tuʻo ua.
Hili ʻene fakatokangaʻi ʻene fehalaakí, koeʻuhi ko ʻene ongoʻi "taʻefiemālié" ne tuli ʻe Plasco-Flaxman ʻa Ms. Maurice, ʻo pehē ko ʻenau neni ʻoku mavahé, ko ha taha ʻAfilika-ʻAmelika, kuó ne fakahoko ha ngāue pango pea ʻokú ne ʻamanaki atu ki ha taha Filipino, ʻo fakatatau mo e New York Post.
Ne totongiʻi ʻa Ms. Maurice ki heʻene ngāue ʻaho tahá pea ne fakafoki ia ki hono ʻapí ʻi ha Uber.
ʻI he taimi ní, ʻoku fakaʻilo ai ʻe Maurice ʻa e ongomātuʻá ki ha totongi huhuʻi ʻo hono tulí, pea ʻokú ne fiemaʻu ha totongi huhuʻi ki he makatuʻunga hono tulí ʻaki ha paʻanga ʻe $350 ki he ʻaho kotoa ʻo ha māhina ʻe 6, ne ʻuluaki fakangāueʻi ia ke livi ʻini, neongo ne ʻikai haʻane aleapau.
"ʻOku ou fiemaʻu pē ke u fakahā kia kinaua ʻoku ʻikai tonu ke ngāue pehē," naʻá ne fakahā ki he Post ʻi he ʻaho Falaité, naʻá ne tānaki atu "ʻOku ou ʻilo ko e ngāue taʻe totonu eni."
Ne toe angatuʻu atu ʻa e ongomātuʻá koeʻuhi ko hona ngaahi talatalaakiʻí ʻo tala ʻoku na laulanu, naʻá na pehē ko hono fakangata ʻo e ngāue ʻa Maurice ne ʻuhinga mālie pē ia, ʻi heʻena hohaʻa ʻe ʻikai te na toe falala ki ia koeʻuhi ko fakamamahi nena fai ki aí.
"Ne ʻave ʻe hoku uaifí ki ai ha meʻa ne ʻikai ke ne ʻuhinga ke lea ʻaki.
ʻOku ʻikai ko ha taha laulanu ia.
ʻOku ʻikai ko ha kakai laulanu ki maua," ne fakahā ʻe he husepānití Joel Plasco ki he Post.
"Ka te ke tuku ho fanaú ʻi he nima ʻo ha taha naʻá ke angakovi ki ai, neongo ko ha fehālaaki pē ia?
Hoʻo pēpē ne toki fāʻeleʻí?
ʻOku hā"
Ko e fakaʻiló ko ha "fakamanamana," ne pehē ʻe Plasco ko hono uaifí ne toki fāʻele pē ʻi ha māhina ʻe ua mei ai pea ʻoku ʻi ham"tuʻunga faingataʻa moʻoni."
"Te ke tuli mui ʻi ha tokotaha pehē?
ʻOku ʻikai ko ha meʻa lelei ia ke fai," ko e tānaki atu ia ʻa e tangata ngāue ʻinivesi pangikeé.
Lolotonga ʻa e ngaahi hopo fakalaó, ne vave ʻa hono tuku mai e fakakaukau ʻa e fakamaauʻanga ʻa e kakaí fekauʻaki mo e ongo mātuʻá ʻi he mītia fakasōsialé, ʻo ta palasia ai ki naua ʻi hona ʻulungaangá mo e fakakakaú.
Hohaʻa ʻa e kau fai pulusi ʻo e Paddington naʻa ʻikai lava ʻa e kau laú ʻo fakahoa ki he pea ʻoku leá, ko e fakahā ia ʻe he tohi foʻoú
Ne fakamatala e ʻofefine ʻo Bond ko Karen Jankel ʻa ia ne faʻeleʻi ʻi ha kiʻi taimi nounou hili hono tali ʻo e tohí, naʻá ne pehē ʻi heʻene tohí: "ʻOku faingataʻa ke fokotuʻu ha taha ʻi he sū ʻo ha taha ʻoku ne lau ia ʻi he fuofua taimí ki muʻa pea toki pulusí.
ʻOku fakafiefia ke ʻilo he taimí ni ʻa e meʻa ʻoku tau ʻilo kau ki he lavameʻa lahi ʻa e Paddington."
Naʻá ne pehē ko ʻene tamaí, ʻa ia naʻá ne ngāue ko ha tangata faitā maʻá e BBC ki muʻa pea ueʻi ia ke ne tohi ʻa e tohi talanoa ʻa e longaʻi fānaú ʻo ha kiʻi meʻavaʻinga pea, mahalo naʻá ne kei vilitaki pē hili ʻa e ʻikai tali ʻene ngāué, naʻá ne tānaki atu ko e taʻu 60 ʻo hono fakamanatua ʻo e pulusinga ʻo e tohí naʻe "ʻikai fuʻu fakafiefia" hili ʻene pekia ʻi he taʻu kuoʻosí.
Naʻá ne fakamatala kau kia Paddington ko ha "mēmipa mahuʻinga ia homau fāmilí naʻá ne tānaki atu ko ʻene tamaí naʻe faʻa fiefia fakalongolongo pē ʻi heʻene lavameʻá.
"Ko ha tangata anga fakalongolongo ia, naʻe ʻikai ko ha tangata polepole," naʻá ne pehē.
"Ka koeʻuhi ne moʻui ʻa Paddington ki heʻene vakaí, ne hangē pē ko ha ʻi ai haʻo leka ʻokú ne lavameʻa: ʻokú ke polepole ʻi ai neongo ʻoku ʻikai ko haʻo ngāue ia.
ʻOku ou tui naʻá ne pehē ʻene vakai ki he lavameʻa ʻa Paddinton ʻi ha founga tatau.
Neongo ko ʻene faʻu mo ʻene fakakaukau, naʻá ne faʻa foaki ʻa e langilangi kia Paddington."
Ne mei mate hoku ʻofefiné pea ne u fiemaʻu ke fai ʻeku lea māvaé ki ai ʻi he telefoní
ʻI heʻene taú pē ne leleakiʻi ai pē hono ʻofefiné ki he Falemahaki Nice's Louis Pasteur 2, ʻa ia ne ngāue ai ʻa e kau toketaá ke fakamoʻui ia.
"Ne toutou tā maʻu pē ʻa Nad ʻo talamai ʻoku fakaʻau ke kovi ange, pea ne ʻikai ha ʻamanaki ʻe taulanga," ko e lau ia ʻa Mrs Ednan-Laperouse.
"Pea ne u maʻu ha telefoni meí a Nad ʻo pehē ʻe mate ia ʻi he ngaahi miniti ʻe ua ka hokó pea kuo pau keu lea māvae ki ai.
Pea ne u fai ia.
Ne u talaange, "Tashi, ʻoku ou ʻofa lahi atu, ʻofaʻanga.
Te u ʻi hena he vave taha.
Te u ʻi hena mo koe.
Ko e faitoʻo ne ʻai ki ai ʻe he kau toketaa ke tokoni ki hono pamu hono mafú ne fakaʻau pē ke holo pea hū ki tuʻa mei hono sinó.
Kuó ne mate ʻi ha ngaahi taimi ki muʻa pea ko ʻeni ne matuʻaki mate.
Ne pau pē keu matuʻaki taʻutu ai ʻo tali, ne u ʻilo kuo kamata ke mahino mai.
Ne ʻikai lava keu fakafoa pe kaikaila pe tangi koeʻuhi ne u ʻi ha tuʻunga ne takatakaiʻi au ʻe ha ngaahi fāmili pea mo ha kakai.
Ne pau ke u loto lahi."
Ne ʻalu pe taimi pea ne tangi ʻa Mrs Ednan-Laperouse ʻi he mole hono ʻofefiná, naʻá ne heka ki he vakapuná fakataha mo e kau pāsesé ʻo ʻikai ha ʻilo ki he hokohoko ʻo e mea ʻoku ne aʻusiá.
"Ne ʻikai ʻilo ia ʻe ha taha," ko ʻene lea ia.
"Ne u punopunou pē, pea ne ʻalu noa pē hoku loʻimatá ʻi he taimí kakato.
ʻOku faingataʻa ke fakamatalaʻi, ka ne u ongoʻi e taulofuʻu ʻo e ongo e mole ʻa Nad ʻi heʻeku puna ko iá.
Naʻá ne fiemaʻu ʻeku ʻofá mo e mahinó.
Ne u ʻilo ʻa e lahi ʻene ʻofa aí."
Ne fakapipiki ʻe ha kakai fefine ha ngaahi kaati ke taʻofi ʻa e taunakita ʻi he hala fakakavakavá
ʻOku ngāue ha ongo fefine ne mālōlō hona ngaahi ʻofaʻanga ʻi he taunakita ke taʻofi ʻa e niʻihi kehé mei hono toʻo ʻenau moʻuí.
Kuo fakapipiki ʻe Sharon Davis mo Kelly Humphrey ha ngaahi kaati popoaki ʻi ha hala fakakavakava ʻi Uēlesi mo ha ngaahi ʻo ha ngaahi pōpoaki ueʻi loto mo ha ngaahi fika telefoni ʻe lava e kakaí ʻo tā ki ai ki ha poupou.
Ne taʻu 13 e foha ʻo Ms Davis ko Tyler ʻi he kamata ke ongoʻi puputuʻu ʻo ne tamateʻi ia ʻi hono taʻu 18.
"ʻOku ʻikai ke u loto ke ongoʻi pehē ha mātuʻa ʻo hangē ko ia ʻoku ou ongoʻi he ʻaho kotoá," ko ʻene vahevahé ia.
Ne pehē ʻe Ms Davis, taʻu 45 ʻoku nofo ʻi Lydney, ne fakatuʻamelie hono foha ke hoko ko ha taha kuki pea mo ha malimali fakatoʻoa loto.
"Ne ʻiloʻi ʻaki ia ʻe he taha kotoa pē ʻaki ʻene malimalí.
Ne nau faʻa pehē ko ʻene malimalí ʻoku ne fakamaamaʻi ha faʻahinga loki pē."
Kaikehe, naʻá ne tukuange ʻene ngāué ki muʻa pea pekiá, he naʻe "ʻi ha feituʻu fakapoʻuli."
ʻI he 2014, ne taʻu 11 ai ʻa e tokoua ʻo Tyler, ko ia naʻá ne faʻa fakasio hono ngaahi tokoua mo e tuofefiné hili ʻene toʻo ʻene moʻuí.
Ne pehē ʻe Ms Davis: "Ne u faʻa hohaʻa maʻu pē ʻo pehē ʻe ʻi ai ha tuktuki."
Naʻe faʻu ʻe Ms David ʻa e ngaahi kaatí, "ke ʻilo ʻe he kakaí ʻoku ʻi ai ha kakai te ke lava ʻo ʻalu ki ai pea mo talanoa ki ai, ʻo tatau ai pē pe ko ha kaungāmeʻa.
ʻOua te ke taʻutu fakalongolongó - ʻoku fiemaʻu ke ke lea."
Ko Ms Humphreys, ʻa ia naʻe kaungāmeʻa mo Ms Davies ʻi ha ngaahi taʻu, ne mali ʻa Mark, ko hono hoa ʻi he taʻu ʻe 15, ʻo ʻikai fuʻu mamaʻo meí he mālōlō ʻene faʻeé.
"Naʻe ʻikai pē te ne talamai naʻá ne ongoʻi lotomamahi mo lotomafasia pe ha meʻa pē," naʻá ne pehē.
"Ne mau fakatokangaʻi ha liliu ʻi heʻene toʻongá ʻi ha ngaahi ʻaho ki muʻa ʻi he Kilisimasí.
Naʻe fuʻu matuʻaki faingataʻaʻia ʻaupito ʻi he ʻAho Kilisimasí - ʻi heʻene fakaava mo e kauleká ʻenau ngaahi meʻaʻofá ne ʻikai ke sio ki honau matá."
Naʻá ne pehē ko ʻene mate ko ha faingataʻa lahi ia kia kinautolu, ka kuo pau ke nau ngāue ke lavaʻi ia: "ʻOkú ne haeʻi ha ava ʻi he fāmilí.
ʻOkú ne fakamavaheʻi kimautolu.
Ka kuo pau ke mau hoko atu pea tau."
Ka ʻokú ke faingataʻaʻia ke hoko atu, te ke lava ʻo tā ki he Samaletani taʻetotongí ʻi he fika ko e 116 123 (UK and Ireland), email jo@samaritans.org, pe vakai ki he uepisaiti ʻa e Samaritans ʻi heni.
Ko e kahaʻ ʻo Kavanaugh ʻoku tautau ʻi he palanisí ʻi he kamata ʻa e fakatotolo ʻa e kau FBI
"Ne u fakakaukau, kapau te tau lava ke maʻu ha meʻa ʻo hangē ko e meʻa naʻá ne kolé - ko ha fakatotolo ne fakangatangata ʻi he taimí, fakangatangata ʻi he lahi ʻo e meʻá - te tau lava pē mahalo ke ʻomi ha kiʻi faaitaha," ne lea ʻaki ʻe Mr Flake ʻi he Tokonakí, ʻo tanaki atu ʻa ʻene manavahē ki he tukupā naʻe "holofā" lolotonga ʻa e mālohi ʻo e fakafaʻafaʻahí.
Ko e hā ne ʻikai fiemaʻu ai ʻe Mr Kavanaugh pea mo hono kaku poupou Lepapuliká ke fakatotolo e kau FBI?
Ko ʻenau taʻeloto ne makatuʻunga ʻi he taimí.
Ko e fili vaeua teemí ʻoku fai ia ʻi ha uike ʻe nima mei heni, ʻi he ʻaho 6 Novema - kapau, ʻe hangē ko e ʻamanakí, ko e kau Lepapulika ʻoku nau fuʻu fakaʻamu ki ai, pea tenau matuʻaki vaivai ʻi heʻenau feinga ke maʻu ʻa e tangata ʻok nau fiemaʻu ke fili ki he fakamaauʻanga maʻolunga taha ʻi he fonuá.
Kuo toʻo ʻe George W. Bush ʻa e telefoní ke tā ki he kau Senatoá, mo fakalotoa kinautolu ke nau poupou kia Mr Kavanaugh, ʻa ia ne ngāue ʻi he White House maʻa Mr Bush pea ne tupunga ʻi ai ʻene fetaulaki mo hono uaifi ko Ashley, ʻa ia ko e sekelitali fakatāutaha ʻa Mr Bush.
Ko e hā ʻa e meʻa ne hoko hili ʻa e faʻu ʻe he FBI ʻene lipootí?
ʻE fai ʻa e fili ʻi he Senató, ʻa ia ʻoku tangutu mei ai ha kau Lepapulika ʻe toko 51 pea Temokalati ʻe 49.
ʻOku ʻikai mahino pe ʻe lava ʻa Mr Kavanaugh ke maʻu ha kiʻi fili ʻikai siʻi hifo ʻi he 50 ʻi he Senato, ʻa ia te ne lava ʻo fakaʻatā ʻa Mike Pence, ko e tokoni palesitení, ke maumauʻi ʻa e mahangá pea fakapapauʻi ia ki he Fakamaau Lahí
'Holo' e fika ʻo e kau hola ʻi he malumalu ʻo Kim
Kuo holo e fika ʻo e kau hola mei Kōlea Tokelau ki Kōlea Tongá talu meí he pule ʻa Kim Jong-un ʻi he taʻu ʻe fitu kuo hilí, ko e lea ia ha taha faʻu lao mei Kōlea Tonga.
Ne fakamatalaʻi ʻe Park Byeong-seug ha fakamatala meí he potungāue fakatahataha ʻa Sauté, ʻo pehē kuo ʻau ki he kau hola ʻe toko 1,127 ʻi he taʻu kuoʻosí ʻo fakatatau ki he toko 2,706 ʻi he 2011.
Ne pehē ʻe Mr Park ko e ngaahi makatuʻungá ʻoku kau ai ʻa hono fusi aʻu ʻo e ngaahi puleʻi ki he kauʻāfonua ʻi he vahaʻa ʻo Kōlea Tokelau mo Siainá pea mo e totongi maʻolunga ʻo e kakai ʻoku nau ʻave fakafūfū e kakaí.
Kuo teʻeki fakahoko ʻe Pyongyang ha fakamatala fakapuleʻanga.
Ko e niʻihi tokolahi ʻo e kau hola mei Noaté ʻoku nau ʻave ha nofo fonua ki Kōlea Tonga.
Pehē ʻe Seoul ne laka hake he toko 30,000 ʻo e kakai ʻo Kōlea Tokelaú kuo nau kolosi taʻefakalao ʻi he kauʻāfonuá talu ʻa e fakaʻosinga ʻo e Tau ʻa Kolea ʻi he 1953.
Ko e tokolahi ʻo e niʻihi ne hola mei Siainá, ʻa ia ʻoku loloa taha honau kauʻāfonua mo Kōlea Tokelaú pea ʻoku faingofua ange ia ki he kolosí ʻi he Sone Maluʻi Taʻemaluʻi ʻe he Sōtiá (DMZ) ʻi he vahaʻa ʻo e ongo Kōleá.
ʻOku pehē ʻe Siaina ko e kau holá ko ha kau hikifonua taʻefakalao ʻo ʻikai ko ha kau kumi hūfanga pea ʻoku faʻa fakafoki nautolu ki honau fonuá.
Ko e vā fengāueʻaki ʻi he vahaʻa ʻo Tokelau mo Tongá - ʻoku na kei tau faka tekinikale - kuo ʻilonga ʻene fakalakalaka ʻi he ngaahi māhina kuo hilí.
ʻI he kamataʻanga ʻo e māhina ní, ne fakataha ʻa e kau taki ʻo e ongo fonuá ʻi Pyongyang ke fakahoko ha talanoa ne fakatefito ʻi he alea ki hono taʻofi ʻo e ngaahi ivi ʻātomí.
Ne hoko ʻeni hili ʻa e fakataha fakahisitōlia ʻi Sune ʻi he vahaʻa ʻo Palesiteni Donald Trump pea mo Kim Jong-un ʻi Singapoa, ʻa ia ne nau felotoi ʻi ha ngaahi makatuʻunga ke ngāue ki muʻa kau ki hono toʻo ʻo e ivi ʻātomi ʻi he peninisulā Koleá.
Ka ʻi he Tokonakí, ne tukuakiʻi ʻe he Minisitā Ki Muli ʻa Kōlea Tokelaú Ri Yong-ho ʻa e fakamanamana ʻa e Puleʻanga ʻAmeliká ki he siʻisiʻi ʻo e fakalakalaká talu mei ai.
"Ka ʻikai ha falala ʻi he Puleʻanga ʻAmeliká ʻe ʻikai ha falala ʻi heʻemau malu fakafonuá pea ʻi he tūkunga ko iá ʻoku ʻikai pē ha founga ia te mau ʻuluaki fakahoko tokotaha hono taʻofi e ngaohi naunau taú," ko e lea ia ʻa Mr Ri ki he Fakatahaʻanga Lahi ʻa e Puleʻanga Fakatahatahá ʻi New York.
Ui ʻe Nancy Pelosi ʻa Brett Kavanaugh ko e "fakaoli," ʻo pehē ʻoku ʻikai taau ia ke ngāue ʻi he Fakamaauʻanga Lahí
Ne ui ʻe he Taki Tokosiʻi ʻo e Falé ko Nancy Pelosi ʻa e tangata fokotuʻu fili ki he Fakamaauʻanga Lahi ko Brett Kavanaugh "fakaoli" pea ne pehē naʻe ʻikai ke taau ia ke ngāue ʻi he Fakamaauʻanga Lahí.
Ne pehē ʻe Pelosi ʻi ha fakaʻekeʻeke ʻi he Tokonakí ʻi he Katoanga Tulaipine ʻi Austin ʻi Texas.
"ʻOku ʻikai lava keu tukunoaʻi ʻa e fakakaukau kapau na ko ha fefina naʻe fakafotunga peheé, te nau pehē 'fakaoli,'" ko e lea ia ʻa Pelosi fekauʻaki mo ʻene ongoʻi ki he fakamoʻoni ʻa Kavanaugh ʻi muʻa he Komiti Fakamaau Senato ʻi he ʻaho Tuʻapulelulú.
Ne fakaʻikaiʻi ʻe Kavanaugh ʻa e tukuakiʻi naʻá ne fakamalohiʻi fakasekisuale ʻa Dr. Christine Blasey Ford ʻi heʻena kei talavou siʻí.
Lolotonga e kamata ʻo ʻene fakamalangá, ne loʻimataʻia ʻa Kavanaugh, ne ai ha ngaahi taimi ne meiei kaila pea faingataʻaʻia ʻi he ʻene fakamatala kau ki hono fāmilí pea mo ʻene ngaahi taʻu ʻi he akoʻanga maʻolungá.
Naʻá ne fakahalaiaʻi ʻa e kau Temokalatí ʻi he ngaahi komití, ʻi heʻenau fakahoko ha tukuakiʻi fekauʻaki mo iá ko ha "palakū, mo ʻulungaanga fakapō" ne fokotuʻutuʻu ʻe he kau lipelolo ne nau ʻita ʻi he foʻi ʻa Hillary Clinton ʻi he fili palesiteni ʻo e 2016.
Ne pehē ʻe Pelosi naʻá ne tui ne fakamahinoʻi ʻe he fakamoʻoni ʻa Kavanaugh ʻe ʻikai ke ne lava ʻo ngāue ʻi he Fakamaauʻanga Lahí, koeʻuhi ʻoku hā naʻe fakapalataha ʻene fehiʻa ki he Temokalatí.
"ʻOku ou tui naʻá ne fakataʻefeʻungaʻi pē ʻe ia ia ʻaki ʻa e ngaahi fakamatalá pea mo e ʻulungaanga ʻa ia naʻá ne lau ai ki he onog Clintons pea mo e Temokālatí," naʻe pehē ʻene leá.
Ne taʻeloto ʻa Pelosi ʻi hono ʻeke atu pe ʻe feinga ke tukuakiʻi ʻa Kavanaugh pe kuo fakapapauʻi, mo e kapau ʻoku tanaki ʻe he kau Temokalatí ʻa e konga lahi ʻi he Fale ʻo e kau Fakafofongá.
"Te u lea ʻaki eni -- kapau ʻoku ʻikai ke ne tala ʻa e moʻoní ki he Fale Aleá pe ki he kau FBI, pea ʻoku ʻikai taau ia ʻo ʻikai ngata pē ʻi he Fakamaau Lahí ka ʻoku tatau pē ki he fakamaauʻanga ʻoku ne ʻi ai he taimi ní," ko e lea ia ʻa Pelosi.
ʻOku lolotonga fakamaau ʻa Kavanaugh ʻi he D.C. Circut Fakamaauʻanga Tangí.
Ne tānaki atu ʻe Pelosi ʻi heʻene hoko ko ha taha Temokalatí ʻokú ne hohaʻa fekauʻaki mo e faingamālia ʻo Kavanaugh ke fai tuʻutuʻuni ki he Lao Tokangaekina Maʻamaʻá pe Roe v. Wade, ʻi he fakakaukau atu ko ha fakamaau molumalu ia.
ʻI heʻene hopo fakapapauʻí, ne kiʻi fakahehema ʻa Kavanaugh ʻi ha ngaahi fehuʻi ʻi he fulihi ha ngaahi tuʻutuʻuni pau ʻi he Fakamaau Lahí.
"ʻOku teʻeki taimi ki ha taha fakaoli, kākā ke ʻalu ki he fakamaauʻangá ʻo ʻamanaki mai ke tau lea ʻo pehē,'ʻikai ko ha meʻa fakaʻofoʻofa iá,'" ko e lea ia ʻa Pelosi.
Pea ʻoku Fiemaʻu ke Puke Ia ʻe he Kakai Fefiné
ʻOku angatonu ke ngāue ki muʻa, ʻi ha ngaahi māhina mo e taʻu ʻo e huaʻi malohí, pea ne ʻikai mei lava ke ne tuku mai ia taʻe tene tangi.
"ʻOku tau tangi ʻi heʻetau ʻitá," ne lea mai ʻaki ʻe Ms Steinem kia au hili ha taʻu ʻe 45.
"ʻOku ʻikai ke u tui ko ha meʻa ia ʻoku ʻikai anga maheni?"
Naʻá ne hoko atu, "Naʻe tokonia lahi au ʻe ha fefine ʻa ia naʻe hoko ko ha pule ʻi he feituʻu, naʻá ne pehē ne tangi ʻi he taimi naʻá ne ʻita ai, ka fakatupulaki ha founga ʻa ia naʻe ʻuhinga ko e taimi ʻok ʻita aí pea kamata ke tangí, ʻe pehē ia ki he taha ne talanoa ki aí, "Mahalo ʻokú ke pehē ʻoku ou loto mamahi ka ʻoku ou tangi.
ʻOku ou ʻita."
Pea naʻá ne hoko atu pē ia.
Ne u fakakaukau ko ha meʻa fakaʻofoʻofa ia."
ʻOku fakaʻatā ʻa e loʻimatá ko ha tukuʻanga ki tuʻa ia ʻo ha ʻita ʻi ha konga koeʻuhi ʻoku faʻa toʻohalaʻi kinautolu.
Ko e taha ʻo ʻeku ngaahi manatu melie lelei tahá ne meí ha ngāue ki muʻa ia, ʻi ha ʻofisi ne fonu ʻi he kakai tangatá, ʻa ia ne u tangi ai ha ʻaho ʻe taha ʻi ha founga loto lili ne ʻikai lava ʻo fakahaaʻi, ne fakafokifā hano haluʻi au ʻi hoku kiá ʻe ha fefine matuʻotuʻa - ko ha pule ngāue anga momoko ʻa ia ne u faʻa ilifia ai - naʻá ne fauʻi au ki he sitepú.
"ʻOua naʻá ke ʻai ke nau ʻilo ʻokú ke tangi," ko ʻene talamaí ia.
"ʻOku ʻikai ke nau ʻilo ʻoku ke fakapoʻuli.
ʻOku nau fakakaukau ʻokú ke loto mamahi pea te nau fiefia ai koeʻuhi ʻoku nau lava ʻo fai ia kia koe."
Patricia Schroeder, ko ha fefine Temokalati mei Colorado, kuo ne ngāue mo Gary Hart ʻi heʻene teu fili fakapalesitení.
ʻI he taʻu 1987, ʻi he taimi ne ʻilo ai ʻa Mr. Hart ʻi ha nonofo kovi ʻi ha vaka ne ui ko e Monkey Business pea tuku ki tuʻa ʻi he lová, ne matuʻaki loto mamahi ʻa Ms Schroeder pea ne pehē ʻoku ʻikai ha ʻuhinga ke ne taʻe ʻahiʻahiʻi ai ʻa e fakakaukau ke lele ki he fili palesiteni maʻana pē.
"Ne ʻikai ko ha fili ne fakakaukauʻi lelei ia," naʻá ne talamai ia kiate au mo ʻene katá ʻi ha taʻu ʻe 30 mei ai.
"Ne ʻosi ʻi ai ha kau kanititeti ʻe toko fitu ʻi he lová, pea ko e meʻa fakaʻosi ne nau fiemaʻú ko ha to e tokotaha.
Ne ui ʻe ha tokotaha ko e "Sinou Uaiti mo e kau ʻInisi Ono ʻe toko Fitú.""
Koeʻuhi naʻe tomui ʻi he kemipeiní, naʻá ne tomui ʻi he tānaki paʻangá, pea naʻá ne tukupā ʻe ʻikai ke kau ki he lová tukukehe haʻá ne tānaki ʻa $2 miliona.
Ne hangē ia ha ulungia ʻi ha taú.
Naʻá ne ʻilo ko e niʻihi ʻo ʻene kau poupoú ne nau ʻave $1,000 ki he kakai tangatá pea $250 pē ki ai.
"ʻOku nau pehē ʻoku ʻou maʻu ha fakamaʻamaʻá?" naʻá ne fifili.
ʻI he taimi naʻá ne fakahoko ai ʻene leá ʻo fakahā ʻe ʻikai ke ne kamataʻi ha kemipeini maau mo fokotuʻutuʻu lelei, naʻá ne ongoʻi taulōfuʻu ʻi he ngaahi ongo ʻo e fakamālōʻia ki he kakai ne nau pououʻi iá, naʻá ne loto mamahi ʻi he sisitemí ʻa ia naʻá ne ngaohi ia ke faingataʻa ke tānaki ha paʻanga pea mo taketiʻi ʻa e kau filí ʻo laka ange ia ʻi he kau fakafofongá, pea mo e ʻita ʻi hono tukuhifo ʻo e kakai fefiné, naʻá ne meimei loʻoa.
"Ne mou mei pehē ne u uesia fakaʻatamai," ko e manatu ia ʻa Ms. Schroeder ki he founga ne fakafotunga ʻaki ʻe he kau fai ongoongo ki aí.
"Ne mou mei pehē ko e Kleenex ʻa ʻeku kautaha poupou fakapaʻangá.
ʻOku ou manatuʻi ʻeku fakakaukau, ko e hā ha meʻa te nau fokotuʻu ʻi hoku maka fakamanatú?
"Naʻe tangí"?""
Ko e founga fakafetongi tau ʻa ʻAmelika-Siaina ʻe ala lelei ki Peisingí
Ko e fana kamata ʻo e fakafetongi tau ʻi he vahaʻa ʻo ʻAmelika mo Siainá ne matuʻaki leʻolahi, pea ʻi he lolotonga ʻa e mamaʻo ʻo e taú mei ha ava ʻi he vahaʻa ʻo e ongo fonuá ʻoku hangē ʻe lelei ia ki Peisingi ʻi he lele lōloá, ne pehē ʻe he kau mataotaó.
Ne tuku atu ʻe Donald Trump, ko e Palesiteni ʻo ʻAmeliká ʻa e ʻuluaki fakatokangá ʻi he kamataʻanga ʻo e taʻu ní ʻaki hono tukuhauʻi ʻa e tefitoʻi fakatau atu ʻa Siainá ʻo fakakau ai mo e sola pēnolo, sitila, mo e ʻalaminiumé.
Ko e matuʻaki hiki lahí ne hoko ia ʻi he uiké ni mo ha tute foʻou naʻá ne uesia ʻa e koloa ne mahuʻingaʻaki ʻa e $200 piliona (£150 piliona), ʻo totongi tukuhau e vaeua ʻo e ngaahi koloa ne ʻomi ki ʻAmelika mei Siainá.
Kuo fakafetau ʻa Peisingi ʻi he taimi kotoa ʻi he fa’ahinga, kimuí ni mai ʻi hono hilifakinga e tute ʻo e peseti ʻe nima ki he hongofulu ʻo e $60 piliona ʻo e koloa ʻAmeliká.
Kuo tukupā ʻa Siaina ke fakatatau ki ʻAmelika, pea ko e fika ua ia ki he ʻekonomika lahi tahá pea ʻoku ʻikai ke nau palani ke kiʻi mālōlō ʻi ha taimi vave mai.
ʻOku ʻuhinga hono feingaʻi ʻo Uasingatoni ke kiʻi tukuloló ki he fiemaʻú, ka punou ki ʻAmeliká ʻe fuʻu fakamā ʻaupito ia ki Xi Jinping, ko e palesiteni ʻo Siainá.
Ka ʻoku kei pehē pe ʻe he kau mataotao kapau ʻe kei lava ʻa Peisingi ke vaʻingaʻi tonu ʻene kaati, ʻe malava ke poupouʻi ʻa Siaina ʻi he taimi lele lōloá ʻaki hono tukuhifo ʻa e fefalalaʻaki ʻa e ongo ʻekonomií.
"Ko e moʻoni ko ia ʻoku lava ʻe he tuʻutuʻuni fakapolitikale vave ʻi Uasingatoni pe Peisingí ʻo faʻu ha tuʻutuʻuni ʻokú ne kamataʻi ha palopalema ʻi he taha pē ʻo e ongo fonuá ʻoku fakatuʻutāmaki ange ia ʻi he sio ki muʻa ʻa e kau mamatá," ne lea ʻaki ʻe Abigail Grace, ko ha tokoni fakatotolo ako ʻoku fakatefito ʻi ʻĒsia ʻi he Senitā ki he Malu Foʻou ʻa ʻAmeliká, ko ha kulupu mataotao ki he palopalema fakaʻekonōmiká.
'Mateuteu' ʻa Syria ke foki mai ʻene kau kumi hūfangá, fakamatala ʻa e Ministiā Ki Mulí
Pehē ʻe Sīlia kuo mateuteu ki he foki tauʻatāina mai ʻo e kau kumi hūfangá pea ʻoku kole ha tokoni ke langa hake ʻa e maumau ʻa e fonuá ʻi ha taʻu lōloa ʻe fitu.
ʻI heʻene fakamatala ki he Fakatahaʻanga Lahi ʻa e Puleʻanga Fakatahatá, ne pehē ʻe he Minisitā Ki Mulí, Walid al-Moualem ʻoku fakalakalaka ʻa e ngaahi makatuʻunga ʻi he fonuá.
"Ko e ʻahó ni ko e tuʻunga ʻo e kelekelé ʻoku toe mālohi pea toe malu fakamālō ki he fakalakalaka kuo fai ʻi hono tauʻi ʻo e tau toitoí," naʻá ne pehē.
ʻOku hokohoko atu ʻa e puleʻanga ki hono fakaakeake ʻa e ngaahi ʻēlia kuo maumauʻi ʻe he kau tau toitoí ke fakafoki ki hono tuʻunga totonú.
Ko e ngaahi makatuʻungá kuo hoko ki he foki tauʻatāina ʻo e kau kole hūfanga ki he fonua ne nau tukuangé koeʻuhi ko e tau toitoí pea mo e tuʻutuʻuni fakaʻekonomiká naʻá ne uesia ʻe nau moʻui fakaʻahó mo ʻenau maʻuʻanga moʻuí.
Kuo fakafuofuoa ʻe he Puleʻanga Fakatahatahá ha kau Sīlia kuo laka hake ʻi he toko 5.5 milioná ne nau hola meí he fonuá talu ʻa e kamataʻanga ʻo e taú ʻi he 2011.
ʻOku kei nofo ha kakai ʻe toko ono miliona ʻi he fonuá ʻoku nau fiemaʻu ha tokoni fakaētangatá.
Kuo fakahā ʻe Al-Moualemʻe talitali ʻe he puleʻanga Sīliá ha tokoni ki hono toe langa honoau puleʻanga maumaú.
Ka ko e kulukiá ʻe malava ke ʻikai ke tali ʻa e makatuʻunga ʻo e tokoní pe tokoni meí he ngaahi fonua ʻoku ne tokoniʻi ʻa e fakafepakí.
Pukepuke ʻe ʻIulopé ʻa e ikuna ʻo e Ipu Ryder ʻi Paris
Kuo malohi ʻa e Timi ʻa ʻIulopé ʻa e Ipu Ryder 2018 ʻi hono ikunaʻi e Timi ʻa USA ʻaki ha kai ko e 16.5 ki he 10.5 ʻi he Malaʻe Tāpulu Fakafonua ʻi tuʻa ʻi Paris, France.
Kuo ulungia hokohoko tuʻo 6 ʻa e US ʻi he konga kelekele ʻo ʻIulopé pea kuo teʻeki ke nau ikunga ʻa e Ipu Ryder ʻi ʻIulope talu meí he 1993.
Kuo toe maʻu ʻe ʻIulope ʻa e kalauní ʻi he aʻu ʻa e kapiteni Tenimaʻake ko Thomas Bjorn ki he poini 14.5 ʻi heʻenau fiemaʻu ke taaʻi ʻa e United States.
Ko e sitā US ko Phil Mickelson, ʻa ia naʻe faingataʻaʻia ʻi he konga lahi ʻo e tunamení, naʻá ne tā lahiʻi ʻene ʻuluaki taá ʻo tō ki he vaí ʻi he pā-3 ava fika 16, ʻo fakaʻatā ai ʻene tau mo Francesco Molinari.
Ne matuʻaki ngingila ʻa e tangata tā pulu ko Molinari ʻi he kotoa ʻo ʻene ʻu vaʻingá, ʻo hoko ko e 1 ʻo e kau vaʻinga ʻe toko 4 ke ʻalu ki he 5-0-0 talu ʻa e tuʻunga tunameni lolotongá ʻi he 1979.
Ne taaʻi ʻa e tangata ʻAmelika ko Jordan Spieth ʻaki ʻa e 5&4 ʻe he tangata vaʻinga ne tuʻunga maʻulalo taha ʻi he timi ʻa ʻIulopé, Thorbjon Olsen ʻo Denmark.
Ko e tangata vaʻinga tuʻunga maʻolunga taha ʻi he māmaní ko Dustin Johnson, ne tō 2 pea 1 kia Ian Poulter ʻo England ʻa ia ʻoku hangē kuó ne vaʻinga ʻi heʻene Ipu Ryder fakaʻosí.
Ko ha tangata vaʻinga fuoloa ʻi ha Ipu Ryder ʻe valu, ko e tangata Sipeini ko Sergio Garcia kuo ne hoko ko e tokotaha taha vaʻinga lelei tahá ʻi he ngaahi tunameni ʻa ʻIulopé ʻaki ha poini ʻe 25.5.
"ʻOku ʻikai ke u faʻa tangi ka ko e ʻaho ni ʻoku ʻikai ke u lava ʻo mapukepuke ia.
Ko ha taʻu faingataʻa.
ʻOku ou houngaʻia kia Thomas ʻi heʻene fili mo falala maí.
ʻOku ou fuʻu fiefia, fiefia lahi ke toe maʻu mai ʻa e ipú.
ʻOku fekauʻaki pe ia moe timí., pea ʻoku ou fiefia ne u lava ʻo tokoni," ko e Garcia ia ʻi he ʻosi ʻa e ikuna ʻa ʻIulopé.
Naʻá ne paasi ʻa e maamá ki hono kaungā fonuá John Ram ʻa ia naʻá ne tuku hifo ʻa e moʻungaʻi fonua ʻAmelika ko Tiger Woods 2&1 ʻi he vaʻinga tāutahá ʻi he ʻaho Sāpaté.
"Ko e polepole ʻoku ou ongoʻí, ke u lakasi ʻa Tiger Woods, he naʻá ku tupu hake ʻo mamata ʻi he tangata ko iá," ko e fakamatala ia ʻa e Rahm taʻu 23.
Ne ulungia ʻa Woods ʻi he fā ʻo ʻene ngaahi vaʻingá ʻi France pea ko ʻeni kuó ne maʻu ha lekooti ʻo e 13-21-3 ʻi he lekooti ʻa e Ipu Ryder.
Ko ha sitetisitika faikehe ʻa ha taha ʻo e kau vaʻinga lelei tahá ʻi heʻene ikuna ha ngaahi hingoa lahi ʻe 14 fika ua atu kia Jack Nicklaus.
Ne faingataʻaʻia ʻa e Timi USA ʻi he kotoa ʻo e fakaʻosinga uiké ke fakasio ha founga lelei tukukehe ʻa Patrick Reed, Justin Thomas, pea mo Tony Finau ʻa ia ne nau vaʻinga ʻi he tuʻunga maʻolungá ʻi he tunamení kotoa.
Ne lea ʻa e kapiteni ʻa e US Jim Furyk hili ha vaʻinga taʻefakafiemālie maʻa ʻene timí, "ʻOku ou polepole ʻi he kau tangatá ni, ʻoku nau tau.
Ne ʻi ai ha taimi ʻi he pongipongí ni ne mau kiʻi laliʻi ʻa Europe.
Ne mau taʻetokanga.
Mālō e vaʻinga Thomas.
Ko ha kapiteni tuʻukimuʻa ia.
Ne vaʻinga lelei ʻene kau vaʻinga ʻe toko 12.
Te mau toe fakataha, te u ngāue mo e PGA ʻa ʻAmeliká mo ʻemau Komiti Ipu Ryder pea temau feinga ki muʻa.
ʻOku ou ʻofeina ʻa e kau tangata ko ʻeni ʻe toko 12 pea kou polepole ke tokoni ko ha kapiteni.
Kuo pau pe ke punou ho’o tātaá.
Ne ʻikai lelei ʻemau vaʻingá."
Fakamuimui Taha mei Tahi Kulokulá: Holo ʻa e lanú ʻi Pinellas, Manatee, pea mo Sarasota
Ko e lipooti foʻou tahá meí he Komisoni Ika mo e Meʻa Moʻuí (FWC) ʻoku hā ai ʻa e holo fakakātoá ʻi he lanu ʻo e Peau Kulokuá ʻi he ngaahi konga ʻo e ʻēlia Tampa Bay.
Fakatatau ki he Komisoni Ika mo e Meʻa Moʻuí, ʻoku lipooti ai ha ngaahi pupunga matala ʻi he ʻēlia ʻo Pinellas, Manatee, Sarasota, Charlotte pea mo ngaahi kolo ʻo Colliers - ʻa ia ʻoku holo ai e lanú.
Ko e matala ʻi he Peau Kulokulá ʻoku ne kapui ha maile fakafuofua ki he 130 ʻo e matāfangá meí he fakatokelau ʻo Pinellas ki he fakatonga ʻo e ngaahi kolo ʻo Lee.
ʻE malava ke maʻu ʻa e ngaahi pupung matalá fakafuofua ki ha maile ʻe 10 meí he matāfanga ʻo Hillsborough County, ka ʻi ha fanga kiʻi feituʻu siʻisiʻi ange ʻi heʻene fakahoa ki he uike kuoʻosí.
Kuo toe lava ʻo siofi ha tahi kulokula ʻi Pasco County.
Ko e lanu ʻikai lahi ʻi loto pea ʻi tuʻa ʻi he matāfanga ʻo Pinella County ʻa ia kuo lipooti ʻi he uike kuoʻosí, ʻa e maʻolunga mo e maʻulalo ʻo e lanú ʻi tuʻa he matāfangá ʻo Hillsborough County, lanu kulokula ʻa e lalo tahí mo e funga tahí ʻi Manatee County, lanu kulokula ʻa e lalo tahi mo e funga tahi ʻo Sarasota County, lanu kulokula lotoloto ʻi Charlotte County, lanu kulokula lalo tahi mo e funga tahi ʻi Lee County, pea lanu kulokula vaivai ʻi Collier County.
ʻOku kei hokohoko e uesia ʻo e halanga mānavá ke lipooti ʻi Pinellas, Manatee, Sarasota, Lee, pea mo e ngaahi kolo ʻo Collier.
Ne ʻikai lipooti ha uesia ʻo e halanga mānavá ʻi he Tokelauhihifo ʻo Florida ʻi he uike kuoʻosí.
